Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
God's Ownership and Our Ownership
Matthew 6:16-34
<Prayer> Father! The time is approaching when our steps must turn toward Heaven. We have come to know the great suffering of the Father, and we understand what the Father's determined will is, and we also know how difficult the responsibility is that the Father wishes us to fulfill as His children. 
We know that those who understand the Father's will, those who will live in the garden that the Father has permitted, must shed infinite tears toward the Father. We understand that when that one person approaches the Father, they cannot help but be wounded, and that person must walk with the Father. We also know that person must bear such marks in their body, and at the same time, they must have a heart full of sorrow and must lament endlessly, preparing for the day of the Father's judgment. Furthermore, we understand that we must be eternally connected with the Father who seeks such sons and daughters. However, today, may we not stand in the position of claiming to be before the Father, and may we not forget that we are those who are ashamed to speak, ashamed to act, and ashamed to lift our faces. 
Now, if there is anyone among us who opens their heart to know the heavenly concerns and to feel the Father's heart, they will be able to weep for the sorrows of the Father and the sorrows of this nation, and they will become friends who can share in the grief that permeates Heaven and Earth with all spirits. 
When we think about whether we stand in such a position today, Father, if we cannot uphold our dignity before the Father who has labored, before the Father who has worried, and before the Father who has walked the path of suffering, may we at least have a heart of remorse. My Father, I earnestly desire and wish for this. 
Father, how great was Your sorrow in leading the chosen people and trying to pass them through the holy city, the gates of Jerusalem? Yet today, we have forgotten Your labor, forgotten Your concerns, and forgotten the footsteps of Your admonitions. Now, if there are movements among the heavenly soldiers, may those movements be steps that follow the Father's footsteps, and may they be movements that advance with pride in their hearts. 
All people do not wish to walk this path. Even today and tomorrow, many people desire this path in their hearts but remain stagnant, unable to connect their actions. Allow us to realize that the responsibility to resolve this does not lie solely with the Father, nor with any leader, but also with us. 
However, we have come to know that very few people are willing to take responsibility for this undeniable fact, so may the Father's earnest heart overflow into our complacent hearts, may the Father's sorrowful heart overflow, and may we become a righteous group that can seek the path of heavenly admonition. Father, I earnestly desire and wish for this. 
Many people wish for heavenly blessings, and many people are trying to be the children of the Father, but in this day, after 6,000 years of history, it is a difficult time to find faithful people who want to be offerings before the Father. We are deeply afraid that we might become a pitiful group that confuses the Father's providential path, so allow us to be those who are concerned about ourselves, like the ancient Israelites, who could not make any guarantees about themselves. 
Today, may we be guided to be diligent sons and daughters who strive not to be children who are ashamed before the Father and who are concerning. Father, I earnestly desire and wish for this. 
At this time, when the grievances of our ancestors block our path, and when countless satans of disbelief are tempting us, may we be allowed to be a valuable existence that can be proudly presented before the Father. Father, I earnestly desire and wish for this. 
We have come out today to worship before the Father, so please allow us to be in a position to establish the conditions of unity and the conditions of goodness that can reflect upon ourselves. Father, who is the group that is praying while worrying about You on this day? Who are those who are shedding tears? Who are those who are grieving on behalf of Heaven and Earth? Please bless them and allow the day of glory to come upon them soon. 
May the sons and daughters gathered here be allowed to take on responsibilities that others cannot bear. May we be true to the remaining mission, faithful to the remaining will, and may we be Your sons and daughters who can fight for the one will of the Father. Father, I earnestly desire and wish for this. 
Today, may we analyze how far our footsteps and our positions are from the original ideal, and may we be led to victory in the fight to break through the standards of concern. 
May everything be fulfilled according to the Father's will on this day. If there are those who have the heart to receive the gift of joy, please work in them, and may You appear as they face the Father and bless them as they earnestly strive for the Father. 
We entrust everything to You, so please take charge. I earnestly ask that this not be a time for Satan to take advantage, and I pray all these words in the name of the Father. Amen. 
<Words> I would like to briefly share some thoughts under the title "God's Ownership and Our Ownership." 
Creatures that have lost their Master
We know that the created beings have lost their Master. We understand that all things are like this, and we ourselves are like this. Due to the fall, humans cannot be absolutely owned by God, nor can they absolutely own all things and this world. And we must recognize this sad fact that even today, the absolute God cannot confidently govern the created things that claim to be His possession. 
Therefore, the historical path until now has been a journey to be owned by one Master. We must keep in mind that we have gone through a tumultuous history of struggles to achieve that purpose until today. 
If we cannot deny the fact that all these created beings exist, then there must be a Master who governs these creatures, some absolute being. Unless we find an absolute point of stability that cannot be slandered under the governance of that absolute being, this world cannot escape the history of struggle. 
Everyone who believes today knows well that God cannot claim the created things He has made as His own. In other words, God is in a position where He cannot govern the things He has created with all His strength according to His will. Therefore, there has been a providential history to restore the original position, and until now, believers have sought God's will while suffering unjust deaths and persecutions throughout the ages. 
The countless children who are fighting to fulfill that one will by being loyal to Heaven and sacrificing their lives for Heaven are also a sorrow for God, as Heaven cannot govern them centered on the ideals of goodness and the glory of victory. And you must understand that this is the sorrow of true people who wish to walk the true path of faith. 
The day when God can boast of the existential value of His ownership before the universe is the day when God's providence is concluded, the focal point of all creation's hope, and the standard that the saints and sages who have come and gone with Jesus have aspired to. 
When you look at your lives and the environment you live in today, can you confidently say whose possessions you have, your own self, your family, your society, and your nation and the world? You cannot say they are the possessions of Heaven, nor can you say they are yours. We must recognize that this has been the greatest sorrow among fallen humanity until now. God could not say to those who wish to follow Him, "Have all the things of the world and follow me." We must feel this situation of God, this extremely sorrowful situation. God should have placed people in the position of the master of all things, yet He cannot urge them to follow Him with everything they have. 
Therefore, those who seek the path of the Way must deeply understand, feel, and experience the sorrowful heart of God, who asks them to forsake all their possessions, their lives, their ideals, and even the joys they can enjoy on this earth. If they do not, they must understand that when the time comes for God's ownership to be recognized, they will have no relationship with God. 
Today, those who claim to believe are saying they want to be saved. They say they want to become people of Heaven. They also have the desire to come forth with the name of the chosen Third Israel. While it is good to have such a heart, you must understand that the issue is whether you have the standards and qualifications to possess it. 
Because Heaven is in a position where it cannot govern all things, no matter how many excellent people have come and gone on this earth, there has never been anyone who could completely govern this earth and determine it as their own. 
So, until when will this historical path continue? The history will continue through twists and turns until the day when a protagonist who can claim this earth as eternally theirs is determined. Until today, humans have boasted that culture, or some political power and religion, are their possessions, but with the changes of the times, the culture that any nation boasted has shifted to another center, and all political powers centered on certain ideologies have changed, and even religions have changed. We can see this well when we examine the historical path. In other words, we can see that no movement has ever stood in a position of decisive ownership. 
The standards of the Way that humans must uphold
The beginning of the fall was when people acted according to their own will at a time when God could not fully govern. Had they acted at a time when God could fully govern, they would not have fallen. Since the creation, God has not been able to exercise His subjective authority. Thus, historically, many people have tried to move nations, states, and the world, but they could not remain as the ones who bore ultimate responsibility for that era. 
Not just individuals, but clans, tribes, nations, and states, and even Heaven and Earth must come under God's governance. Therefore, if there is a heavenly realm, there must be an inevitable movement in the historical end times that governs that realm, or else the overall ideals governed by God cannot be fulfilled. 
Therefore, Heaven is demanding that we humans forsake all material possessions, forsake our lives, forsake our ideals, and even forsake the joys we can enjoy on this earth. This is the standard of the Way that God asserts over humanity. 
So why has God set forth these conditions of demand? It is because the time will inevitably come when the authority of the absolute being's ownership is revealed, and He wants to make us qualified to stand before Him at that time. Thus, this has been an essential condition that those who have followed God and sought the will of goodness must uphold until now. 
Looking back at the history of Christianity, we see that God made people suffer before giving them joy, made them face persecution before allowing them to boast, and urged them to pray without ceasing, avoiding the environment in which they could enjoy themselves. We must understand that God presented these standards of the Way to make humans His complete possession at a certain time. 
In the biblical text, it says, 
"Forsake all and seek the kingdom and its righteousness." Where is that kingdom that can be called God's kingdom, and where is that righteousness that can be claimed as God's? Also, where is the person who can be called a person of God? In other words, what kind of kingdom can God possess? It will be the kingdom of goodness. That kingdom will transcend religion, the concept of a single nation, human discrimination, sovereignty, and any culture or ideology. 
Therefore, Heaven is the place that good people from both East and West have claimed as their ideal nation, the place they wish to live. And Heaven is the place where one can confidently assert their ownership and establish the concept of possession. This is the kind of place we desire Heaven to be. 
Today, whether it is Christianity or any denomination, if there are people who are steeped in a possessive mindset centered on themselves or a denominational ownership concept, then those people...
The time for striking will inevitably come. There will come a time when a certain nation's attention will be focused, drawing together and uniting all of God's possessions and our possessions. This is an ironclad rule.

God even tolerates Satan. So why does God not strike Satan and instead allow him to exist? And what is the reason for listening to Satan's pleas and granting him conditions for accusation? It is because, although Satan opposes God's will and does not follow it, he does not hate God. Although he does not follow God's will, he respects and likes God in his heart.

Satan is pleading with God, saying, "O God! I will give you this world that is in my hands. Therefore, please set me in place of Adam, leaving Adam aside. If you do this for me, I will serve you more than any human." Satan is asking that if God places him in such a position, he will serve God more than humanity.

God is in a difficult position.

God's possessions and Satan's possessions

Then what was the purpose of sending numerous prophets and Jesus from heaven? It was to establish someone who knows God's situation, as much as Satan knows it, and who can act on behalf of God, exercising ownership over Satan. The purpose of the Second Advent is to complete this task.

So what is the motivation behind Satan being Satan? What is the motivation for breaking the heavenly order? It was to receive more of God's love than Adam and Eve. If Adam and Eve had loved God as much as God loved them, and if they had loved God more than anything else, they would not have fallen. This is where the condition lies. What is evil? It is the inability to serve others over oneself and the inability to serve goodness. Today, fallen humanity is caught in this condition.

Then what kind of nation is a good nation? What kind of nation can God possess? What kind of person can be owned by God? What kind of things can be owned by God? The conclusion is that anything centered on oneself cannot be owned by God. It must be a being that stands in a position centered on God, a being that can be absorbed by God. Such beings can be owned by God.

The law of the satanic world is to live for oneself. Therefore, people in the satanic world believe that all existence in families, societies, nations, and the world must exist solely for their own benefit. This is the difference from the law of good, which is God's law. So what is a good person? A person who feels everything they own, even their thoughts, as belonging to others and can use them for others or for the whole.

Thus, in the human world, what kind of phenomena of corruption have occurred? There has been a phenomenon of trying to draw all things, the world, and even God into a life centered on oneself. This is the phenomenon of corruption that arose due to Satan's work.

Then what is the work of goodness? It is a history that causes a revolution within oneself, working for God, for the world, and for others, pioneering a new direction. This is also the purpose of religion.

Therefore, looking back on the history of Christianity, there has never been a person who followed God's will and had God's mission who lived for themselves, regardless of the era or century.

To this day, all the heroes and great figures in the satanic world who lived for themselves have disappeared. Such people are criticized after history passes.

The Principle of Jesus

What was the purpose of Jesus coming to this earth? It was to restore the nation that God can possess, the people that God can possess, and all things that God can possess. And what was the principle he advocated? Jesus' principle was, "Let us sacrifice ourselves and serve the nation, the world, and the universe." Those who serve and sacrifice greatly for the universe become the masters of that universe.

Even today, we can see many such people in the world of evil. We can know that those who serve silently and faithfully become the masters wherever they go, in any nation or society.

Now we must feel the responsibility that it is our duty to find the authority for God to possess my individual self, family, society, nation, world, and universe. This ownership is not established by God Himself but must be established and resolved by humans. Because this significant duty remains, many saints and sages who have represented historical providence have had to face execution and death to fulfill this duty.

Jesus, for over thirty years, worked in Joseph's house and could not claim to be the Son of God. He could not claim to be a being like the ambassador of heaven with full authority. This was because Jesus knew that even God, after a long history, had never made such a claim. Therefore, even in the Garden of Gethsemane, facing the cross, he could not pray centered on his own will, saying, "Father, let it be done," but instead prayed, "Father, not my will, but yours be done."

The more Jesus had a strong sense of mission and responsibility for the earth as the Savior, the stronger his consciousness of existence and ownership would be. However, he knew very well that he should not live only for himself. And Jesus knew that he must be owned by God as God's possession and could feel God's heart while also being able to seek God's will. Thus, he was able to replace God's heart with his own heart and stand in a position where he could replace God's will with his own will. And before all created beings, he could qualify as the Savior who must follow the will of heaven and the heart of heaven.

Qualifications of the Citizens of Heaven

Then what kind of people are the citizens of heaven? They are those who raise the banner of service before all people. Therefore, today, in order to save any nation, we must share everything we own for that nation. If that is not enough, we must be willing to give our very lives. Such people are the citizens of heaven. You must think that God has a situation where He needs to gather such people to fulfill the ideals of heaven.

If we understand that Jesus intended to determine a certain value of ownership on this earth, we must reflect on ourselves. Jesus said, "Do not worry about what you will eat, what you will drink, or what you will wear" (Matthew 6:31). This was a contradictory warning to the people of that time.

So why did he say such words? It is because there remains the ideal of heavenly ownership that must be restored, even if one does not eat, drink, or wear anything for six thousand years.

Even if there is a starving and pitiful nation, God is in a position more pitiful than that nation, and if there is an unjust nation, God is in a position more unjust than that nation.

Yet God cares more for us than we care for ourselves. When we see people who should understand this not understanding and worrying only about their own individual selves, Jesus spoke those words. Therefore, if there is someone who wants to seek that kingdom and its righteousness today, they must raise their voice before heaven, saying, "How many good people are there who are starving like me on this earth?" It is natural for oneself, who is not in a position of goodness, to suffer from hunger, but it should not be that those in the position of goodness are starving. We must be concerned for such people. We must understand that this fate is imposed upon us.

Thus, even if Jesus is in a position where he cannot eat or wear anything, he spoke these words hoping that we would work to create the nation and people that God can possess.

So if God exists, what kind of person will He choose? What kind of person will He choose to be His child? He will seek out that one person who can raise their hand to bless others, surpassing their own hunger and difficulties, and who can cry for God's anger and sorrow, transcending their own anger and sorrow.

Thus, even on the cross, where Jesus' own fate was at stake, he looked at his enemies and could not say, "O heaven! Eternal heaven! Pour out eternal punishment upon them." Instead, he raised his hand and prayed for blessings upon them. You must understand that such a heart of Jesus is the heart of the citizens of heaven and, indeed, the heart of God.

Based on these principles, when we examine our faith life and the Christianity that claims to believe in God today, how many people can remain as citizens of heaven? Furthermore, where is the nation that can eternally claim to be God's possession, and where is the land that can claim to be God's kingdom? Where are such things and such people? You must understand this.

You all desire to go to heaven. Moreover, today we often see people confidently claiming, "Ah! The kingdom is mine." When we see such people, we may wonder how they can speak so boldly about ownership in relation to God.

Even God Himself has not yet stood in a position to claim, "The kingdom is mine," nor has Jesus stood in such a position.

Jesus is still in a position of praying towards heaven. God has also been working until now.

Why is it that the countless spirits in the spiritual world are cooperating for the earth, and why are they not able to enjoy a joyful life in the place of liberation and glory? Why must they stand in such a position? It is because God has not been able to stand in a position to claim, "I have established the kingdom since creation." Even though God is in such a position, today, among the saints on earth, some stand in positions that contradict the principles of heaven and make such claims.

The Reason Saints Must Suffer

The more one goes towards heaven, the more one feels the debt they owe. God has been seeking that nation and people for six thousand years. Thus, the historical debt of labor that God has accumulated over six thousand years cannot be claimed to be owned by someone just because they have personal satisfaction and joy.

Therefore, if one is a child of heaven, there remains a land and a world where they have the responsibility to care for God and protect on behalf of God. As long as these things are not able to be owned by God, one must feel that they cannot be confident in themselves.

Thus, Jesus came to this earth with a mental standard that could carry out leading activities as a prince of heaven, but he never exercised that authority. Wherever he went, he washed the feet of his disciples and healed the sick. Therefore, there was not a single day in Jesus' life that he lived for himself.

Looking back on his life, it was solely a life lived for others. It was a life of struggling for others, shedding tears for others, being insulted for others, being torn for others, and being killed for others.

If God cannot resolve this sorrow of Jesus, then such a God is unnecessary. Therefore, until the day comes when we can liberate God from the chains of sorrow and God can raise His hand and say, "The whole heaven and earth are mine! Let us all enjoy together!" we must understand that we cannot claim our own position. And because of this complexity, the truth of Christianity has emphasized love, sacrifice, service, persecution, and a life of being despised.

So how can we become God's possessions? We must be able to shed many tears for God. The more we have the heart to mourn God's sorrow, the more we will become God's possessions, and the more we bear God's suffering, the more we will become God's possessions. The more we are accused by Satan on behalf of God, the more we will be God's possessions.

Therefore, as much as you have acted and been faithful, that is how much you will become God's possessions, and this will not happen in good places but will occur when you hold on to the sorrows and pains that all humans have rejected.

This is the path of principles that Christians must follow.

The reason Christianity ignited in Korea was precisely because the early Christians walked this path. If there had been groups that denied, "If we are citizens of heaven, why do we die?" the providence of God would not have been able to be spread in Korea.

Furthermore, if Jesus Christ Himself had denied, "Why should I, as the Son of God, die? Why should I be insulted and despised?" the path of salvation that you can believe in today would not have appeared in human history.

What was the reason for teaching patriotism as a means of guiding the people in every nation? It was because they set aside their families and their own desires and honors to represent the will of the nation. They took on the suffering of their nation, bore its sorrows, and sought to take responsibility for everything on behalf of the nation's master. You must understand that this is the attitude of keeping the laws of heaven.

In today's chaotic world, many people are trying to assert themselves and show their authority, believing themselves to be superior. It is difficult to find true Christians. It is even more difficult to meet true sons of God, true people whom God can own.

Now we must welcome friends, become citizens of heaven, and form a denomination to organize a tribe.

But where is that one saint who has received the decision of ownership from God in the territory of Korea? Where is that one denomination in the territory of Korea, and where is that one nation in the world? We must realize that the time has come for us to cry out until we exhaust all our energy and to seek until we collapse.

Youth Who Will Save the Nation and the World

Therefore, today you must have a heart that wants to dress up this thirty million people before dressing yourself, a heart that thinks of all people on this earth before thinking of yourself. Furthermore, you must have a heart that can hold onto even a blade of grass and cry for it, a heart that can explode from within without you even knowing it. Without such a heart, you cannot become a complete son or daughter of God.

Because such humans are the fruits of God's tears and the fruits of God's suffering.
This is also a sacrifice that ascends upon the altar of God's blood. Nevertheless, people shamelessly assert themselves without considering this. The same goes for all creation.

So who will pave the way for this nation? A people must arise who truly mourn for this nation, striking the ground and their chests in lamentation. And who will correct this divided denomination? Young men and women with burning passion to hold onto the denomination must be able to strike the ground and appeal, prepared for a bloody battle against the hypocrites.

Then who will save this world? It is you, young men and women. You must think about this once again.

Today, Western material civilization has developed significantly. This has formed Western civilization, starting from continental Egypt, passing through Assyrian civilization, Babylonian civilization, Greek civilization, and Roman civilization, up to the present day.

When we look at religious history, what did the Egyptian nation, which boasted over 3,000 years of civilization during the time of Jesus, center its civilization around? The Egyptians worshipped the sun god and believed in the god Osiris. With this faith and ideology, they armed their spirits and exerted united strength to build such a powerful nation and civilization. They adopted this as a policy ideology, strengthened their rituals, and led their nation toward that ideal standard, giving birth to Egyptian civilization.

Thus, they established what could be claimed as a nation, and by doing so, they gained the criteria to govern. At this time, if they found something good beyond their own nation, they had to absorb that good. If they had sacrificed anything from their own country to accept and change, that nation would not have perished.

However, that nation perished, but their civilization has developed throughout history. In the Orient, Assyrian and Babylonian civilizations arose, while in Palestine, Judaism centered around Hebrewism formed a civilization based on God.

In Greece, the civilization centered on the ideology of external gods developed, eventually harmonizing with various artistic worship movements. This became the unique religious ideology established by the Greeks, which passed through the kingdom of knowledge.

Thus, a global civilization sphere was formed, and during the period of chaotic ideologies, it merged with Christian thought, later crossing over to Rome to establish Christian civilization.

In the Middle Ages, Christianity had to absorb and merge people under the ideology of this religion, regardless of status. However, failing to achieve this purpose and falling into secular corruption led God to strike.

If the Roman Catholic Church had not been corrupt, and if they had the mission that their existence was for the world and for humanity, advocating the idea that they should live for others before themselves, the papacy would not have collapsed.

However, because the Roman Catholic Church failed to do this, God had to intervene externally by initiating the Renaissance and internally by instigating the Reformation against the Catholic Church. Thus, later, centered around the Puritans, they crossed over to the American continent and built a nation centered on Christian ideals. In other words, the political ideology of Rome, the religious ideology of Christianity, and the intellectualism of Greece merged to form the Pan-Americanism that governs today's democracy.

Now, until America integrates today's democracy and can fulfill its national mission and possess the authority to act on behalf of others, what kind of ideology should it have? First, it must abandon the ideology of self-first. This is the most crucial thing for the American people.

Therefore, if America claims that its economy, culture, science, religion, and political system exist solely for its own people, that is correct. Thus, the Renaissance movement arose to awaken, and today, communism is emerging to awaken as well. Now, ideological and religious movements will appear. At such times, we must have the heart of pioneers to discern the heavenly movements.

Where will the religious ideology that can strike America come from? Those with a will must think about this.

This is a historical developmental phenomenon that arises because the absolute ownership rights have not been found, and it is being pushed and pulled to that point.

So what is the Renaissance movement? It was a retro movement of Hellenism, emphasizing the recovery of human nature and self-awareness based on the Greek spirit. Likewise, all Christianity within the democratic sphere centered around America must return to the spirit of early Christianity. We must not only believe in the revealed word but also seek the ideologies contained within the word and initiate a rearmament movement centered around that. If we fail to do so, contemporary Christianity will stand in the same position as the medieval Catholic Church.

Why is that? Because it is not God's word that is required, but God's people, God's nation, and God's kingdom that are required. The word has come for that purpose.

Now is the time to move beyond the era of absolute words and build the era of absolute reality. Therefore, the historical end time of the era of passing through words is coming. And this era is called the judgment era.

When we think about this, history is ringing an alarm for us today. The footsteps of the prophets and sages of the past are moving our lives, and their spirit is adjusting our thoughts from behind. Therefore, those who deviate from this will inevitably face a major surgery according to heavenly law.

Then, after God finds the land and the people of the land and makes them heavenly, what should happen? We must welcome the day when we can boast of God's life as our own. We must welcome the day when we can boast of God's ideals and love before the universe and humanity.

So, is there anyone among you today who has boasted of God's life? If so, come forward. Is there anyone who has been willing to sacrifice their life to establish the glorious heavenly kingdom? If so, come forward. And is there anyone who has come forth to build heaven on earth to become a true child of God?

Many may have tasted the flavor of heaven while being within the realm of Satan's accusations during the restoration process, but no one has truly experienced the taste of the eternal peaceful homeland, heaven, after removing Satan. Those who have truly felt the taste of heaven and God's love are stimulated to fight against Satan. And once someone has felt the true taste of heaven and received God's love, they will never depart from God again. Thus, those who have experienced God's love must appear on this earth.

Then, what is the limit where God's ownership must be determined? It starts from a single blade of grass, from a single pyeong of land, from one person, starting from the very end and reaching up to heaven, and furthermore, to God's heart world.

However, the form of that ownership must not be relative or conceptual. It must be subjective and objective. Only when such a world is built can God's rest be achieved.

What God likes, humans cannot dislike. For this reason, God designated the seventh day as a day of rest and commanded to rest. However, have you realized that God has not been able to boast of resting until today, after 6,000 years of history? Did you realize that?

Jesus also emphasized the word of the gospel and the importance of the Sabbath, holding onto the history of struggle within the twists and turns of 2,000 years of providential history, but has there ever been a day when he could boast to the Father and rest with all people in glory? There has not been. Because God and Jesus are in a position where they cannot rest, we also cannot rest.

For this reason, there will be wars before rest comes, there will be suffering before rest comes, and there will be death before rest comes. Only when we overcome and surpass this can we even taste the flavor of rest. Jesus also felt one aspect of rest after the cross, but only after going through such a path.

So now, what should we possess? We must possess the garden of rest, the garden of happiness, the garden of goodness, the garden of love, and the garden of ideals. However, before possessing this, we must first be beaten by Satan and also beaten by heaven. Jesus was also beaten by Satan and heaven. The Pharisees of Judaism drove Jesus out, and at the same time, the Romans drove him out. Then, when Jesus was about to die on the cross, he earnestly prayed, "My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?" (Matthew 27:46), indicating that even God had forsaken him.

Therefore, the person who will possess heaven, the person who can be possessed by heaven, is the one who finds God and is placed in the most pitiful position because of God. Among all humanity, which nation can possess God? It is the most pitiful nation. The more pitiful the nation, the closer it is to God.

Therefore, in the end days, a great tribulation will come. What does this mean? Let us establish the welfare that God wishes to govern
God has been introducing the truth through Christianity until now. He has given the word to restore reality to humans, but the mission of that word has not been completed, and history continues to flow.
Two thousand years ago, Jesus came to this earth to complete the mission of that word and to bring about a revolution of the heart and emotion, but because humans did not believe in and welcome Jesus, these things could not be realized. Therefore, today these things remain to be raised again before humanity.
Not only the Christian believers who believe in Jesus but also countless other religious people are longing for such a true word. If a word of truth that can restore fallen humans, encompassing body, mind, and emotion, comes forth, the world will naturally be unified. There must be a providence of restoration to save fallen humans, and there must be an internal revolution to reclaim what has been lost due to the fall. The people who must carry out this internal revolution are the Christians of the last days, religious people, and conscientious individuals. In fact, conscientious individuals do not make a significant contribution to God’s providence of restoration. No matter how much they suffer, the end times are coming.
In this light, the words of the 66 books of the Bible are precious. However, through the Bible, it is difficult to evoke the original heart of humans and to stimulate the original emotions. Therefore, we must seek a new word that encompasses these two contents.
If we cannot find such a word, God’s 6,000-year providential history will return to failure. When we see such a phenomenon, in order to prevent God’s providence of restoration from failing, considering the trend of history where the cultures and thoughts of the world are converging, what is absolutely necessary in these last days is a word that can move the original heart and the original emotion. This is the issue.
Two thousand years ago, Jesus Christ who came to this earth could not say all that he wanted to say. He also wanted to love humans but could not love them all. This was a great sorrow for humanity. And it was also a sorrow for God.
For humans on the path of restoration, the inability to introduce the world of body and mind, the world of emotion, and the heart of God was the sorrow of God and the sorrow of Jesus.
We must understand the hearts of God and Jesus
So, today as we seek that word, God is not a being who exists beyond the universe. Creation cannot achieve completion without a relationship and connection with God. Even when we build a house, we must connect all the materials and have interrelations to complete the house.
Now, we must find the heart and emotion of God among the 66 books of the Bible, and we must find the heart and emotion of Jesus. Only by understanding the hearts and emotions of God and Jesus can we understand our own hearts and emotions. However, the Bible does not fully express the heart and emotion of God and the heart and emotion of Jesus. The Bible records that “Heaven is in your heart,” but how many people can truly say that heaven is in their heart? Where are such people…
We, who must find such things today, when we think about it, there are many who can recite good Bible verses, excellent phrases. Now, to know the heart and emotion of Jesus, we must understand why Jesus, who came as the Savior of all mankind and the true Father of all, was sorrowful on this earth, and what he was most sorrowful about. We must know this. Only by knowing this can we say that we understand the heart and emotion of Jesus. We must understand what Jesus felt most wronged, indignant, and pained about, and what the circumstances were.
Then, regarding Jesus, we must say, “Is your heart and emotion like this? I understand that heart and emotion.” We must be able to comfort Jesus. Only then can we truly become a human being. You must understand this.
Let us establish the welfare that God wishes to govern
God has been sorrowful and has suffered throughout history to find even one human being. We must understand that the historical content has been like this, the content of the times has been like this, and furthermore, the hope for the future is like this. Because we do not know this, humanity is struggling today all over the world.
After Jesus walked the path of sorrow, the path of suffering, and the path of the cross on this earth, he welcomed a joyful day of resurrection, but while he could rejoice regarding heaven, he could not rejoice regarding the humans on earth. You must understand this.
Then why was it that Jesus, who welcomed the day of resurrection, could say, “Father!” to God and rejoice, but could not rejoice regarding humans? Jesus knew the heart of God and understood the emotion of God.
Thus, holding onto the heart of God and the emotion of God, he could weep, give thanks, and rejoice. However, there was not a single person among the humans on earth who could hold onto such Jesus and rejoice. That is why Jesus could not rejoice regarding humans. If humans could have attended and enjoyed the place where heaven rejoices in the glory of resurrection, the sorrowful historical process of 2,000 years would not have unfolded.
With this emotional context, the resurrected Jesus was seen by Mary Magdalene, and when she tried to hold onto him saying, “Oh Lord!” Jesus said, “Do not hold onto me.” What does this mean? No matter how much humans try to hold onto Jesus, they cannot become one with him without knowing his sorrow and pain, and without understanding his heart and emotion.
Now, humans living on this earth must abandon the material and the way they possess. What kind of people were those who opposed Jesus?
We must learn to abandon all the material we possess, all the ideologies we hold, and everything we have to seek to understand the heart of Jesus. The heart of Jesus was not a heart that sought for himself, but a heart that sought for God. And he sought to hold the heart of God in his heart.
In order for God and Jesus to rejoice
God’s heart had a course of twists and turns. Jesus explained this, saying, “God! Now I understand. I have come to know what your ultimate purpose is and what kind of heart you have while governing.” He held onto God, forgetting his own dignity and face, and wept and rejoiced. Just as Jesus did, you too must be able to hold onto Jesus and weep and rejoice. Only then can the ideals of the inner world manifest in the outer world. You must understand this.
This is the core of faith, so even if humans raise both hands to believe in the Lord, practice the word with love, and restore reality with faith, what remains in the end is the unification of God’s heart, Jesus’ heart, and human hearts, and furthermore, the unification of God’s love, Jesus’ love, and human love. This is the ultimate task and static task of believers. That is why the religion of Christianity, which is a religion of love, is the one that remains in the end. The people of heaven are those who struggle to give. They are those who struggle to give their body, mind, and all of themselves. However, most people in this fallen world are those who struggle to live centered on themselves. Such people must be able to bring about a revolution of the heart to become sons and daughters who can receive God’s love, who wishes to create and embrace all creation and love it.
Until now, God has never embraced and loved a person who has fulfilled the condition of both spirit and flesh. Jesus also could not love such a person. That is why Jesus is still praying in paradise.
For this reason, we must long only for the love of God, who wishes to embrace our spirit and flesh, and we must receive the love of God, which does not matter compared to the love of a parent for a child, and only then can we establish the justification of being a child of God and govern all things. You must understand that this world is the world that God wishes to restore and the garden of rest.
Now, returning to the issue of our individual selves, what should we, who are placed in the destiny of restoration, do? We must seek a new ideology. The time has come for that. In the future, the issues of true views on life and the universe will arise. The worldview based on the recognition and concepts of the visible material world will be transcended. We will pioneer the invisible world through the recognition of the world of the heart and the feelings we experience.
If a universal ideology that can integrate the world of the heart emerges on this earth today, that ideology will be the last ideology. After that, there will be only love.
Today, scientific civilization has developed to an extreme. However, we must enhance the level of spiritual civilization so that it can govern this scientific civilization. We must surely find any ideology that can govern the world of the heart and further the world of the spirit. Finding such an ideology is our destiny. You must certainly understand this.
Thus, we must be connected to God’s love. God’s love is a love through the universe, and if we hold onto that love, the entire universe can enter into us. We must become sons and daughters who can feel such universal emotions, represent all creation, sing before heaven, and live joyfully with heaven. Furthermore, we must become sons and daughters who possess the authority to govern all things. Only by becoming such sons and daughters can we be recognized as children who can live in the ideal garden of God’s creation and be embraced and loved by God. You must understand this.
<Prayer> Father, although humans do not know the flow of history, we know that you have personally managed the will of providence.
Today, let your sons and daughters who have come here be allowed to critically examine what kind of environment they are in. Is there anyone living to find their body, seeking the rest of their body? Is there anyone living only for the rest of their heart? We earnestly wish and hope that you will allow us to be sons and daughters who can find rest through your love, transcending these things.
We have come to understand that this is the inevitable path of restoration that humans must take. Because we have lost this due to the fall, please allow us to rise boldly before the history of humanity that has wandered in search of faith, reality, words, and love, and to stand proudly before all creation on this earth with a heavenly heart, heavenly love, and heavenly desire.
Father, we earnestly ask that you eternally embrace our body and heart with eternal life, and we pray all these words in your name. Amen. 
3) Humanity wandering in search of the truth
Matthew 7:1-12
<Prayer (I)> Beloved Father, as we look at the ideal garden of love, we should admire your love, but after rejecting your heart that wishes to build the ideal garden of love, we have left behind a trail of sorrowful tears over thousands of years of historical progress. Please allow us to accept such humans.
It is time to long for the lost love of the Father, and we know that the end of restoration is approaching, and we must stand on the side of the Father by tracing the Father’s heart. Beloved Father, please establish us today and renew us. Since you have called us, please guide us anew. We earnestly wish and hope that you will allow us to be those who can worship before you with joy and glory, having removed the sorrows of restoration.
Now, please do not allow our hearts to remain only in our hearts, and do not allow our bodies to become only our own bodies. Please do not allow everything from the emotions we feel to the concepts or claims we hold to become ours. We know that nothing that started from us is ours, and that everything is a fact that has come to be based on heaven. Therefore, at this time, please allow us to be those who can present everything as yours and return everything to you, beloved Father, we earnestly wish and hope.
Even if we claim to have our own minds, we cannot appear before all creation with only that mind, and even if we have our bodies, we cannot proudly appear before all people. Please allow us to understand that we cannot boast before the universe with anything we possess. Thus, let us give up everything and receive the heart of resurrection from the Father and be transformed into the heart of the Father, and guide us to be able to enter into the heart of the Father. We earnestly wish and hope for a heart that can receive the command of re-creation with a heart of joy, beloved Father.
Father, as the little ones have gathered for this hour, please govern the hearts we have brought. It is our duty to offer gifts when we bow before your presence, but we have come without bringing anything.
Please forgive me. What I can offer before the Father is only a sincere heart.  
Please accept this heart as Yours, and I dedicate this body to You,  
that it may become a living sacrifice. May this earnest heart and longing  
be manifested upon the heads of all gathered here, upon their hearts,  
and upon their minds. I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.  
Father! Please govern the hearts of Your sons and daughters gathered here.  
Each individual is different, and thus their circumstances will differ,  
the emotions they feel will differ, the struggles of the past will differ,  
and their claims will differ, so their understanding will also differ.  
But for this one hour, may we be held in Your heart,  
and may we be governed by Your earnest heart.  
And may You bind us together as one,  
allowing us to become a sacrifice for one purpose.  
I ask that there be no one among this audience  
who has a heart that can be exploited by Satan.  
Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.  
Father, I thank You for the framework You have allowed us,  
and we come to realize the mission we must take responsibility for.  
Father, we have proclaimed Your word before this nation,  
so please allow many to appear with a longing heart toward Heaven  
because of this word. Among this nation,  
may there be many who hold onto this word and earnestly pray toward You.  
As we stand at the end times,

to fulfill the glory and will of Heaven,

I believe that it is not difficult for Your glory to bear fruit.  
I earnestly hope and wish that we may be faithful in preparing for this,  
both internally and externally, Father.  
Now, please allow us to recognize that this is a time  
when we must devote our hearts and bodies to prayer,  
and allow us to carry the words we need to convey in our hearts and bodies.  
If we do not lose the responsible heart to practice these words,  
I know that the fruits will appear before this nation.  
Father, please fulfill Your will through this nation,  
and I earnestly hope and wish that You receive the glory through this nation.  
This day is a holy day, the day You promised to bless all people,  
so please bless every altar where we kneel earnestly toward You.  
We are children gathered here in the name of the Son,  
connected through one heart and one blood,  
so please allow us to become one with each other.  
Please allow us to accept each other,  
and help us to unite with one another.  
Thus, may we also embrace the heart that You hold,  
and may we become a group that can care for Your will.  
Father, have mercy on the Korean church.  
They are seeking the path of life,  
but they do not know where to go,  
and even if they do not have confidence in their own lives,  
please bless that denomination.  
Father, please shine the light of life upon those who wander,  
not knowing where to go.  
Please allow this nation to be one that can boast  
before all people as Your sons and daughters,  
revealing the glory of victory before all creation.  
Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.  
Father, we understand that You have driven us to a lonely place  
for a great providence.  
Please allow us to become a sacrifice before the nation.  
The duty of a sacrifice is to first please You,  
and only then should all things rejoice.  
Therefore, the sacrifice must live devotedly for Your will,  
and the sons and daughters gathered here also understand this.  
Now, in accordance with the heavenly heart You have established,  
may this one body and heart become an altar,  
and may this body and heart be a sacrifice offered before You.  
May this one body become the substantial temple of the Father,  
able to sing of Your glory,  
and may we become sons and daughters who can comfort Your heart alone,  
I earnestly hope and wish for this, beloved Father.  
On this day, please be with Your sons and daughters  
who are fighting to fulfill their responsibilities  
amidst various persecutions and difficulties.  
If You have led them out,  
please guide their fruits to be realized in Your embrace,  
I earnestly hope and wish for this, Father.  
Now, I lay this inadequate sincerity before You,  
so if there is any lack, please personally strike it with a whip.  
Still, if there are children who can understand Your heart,  
please allow this hour to be one where we can express  
Your circumstances and Your heart.  
I earnestly ask and wish for this.  
Please take charge of all that happens today.  
I pray in the name of the Lord. Amen.

Hearts must connect with hearts,

<Prayer (III)> Father, please transform our hearts into empty hearts.  
Please allow our hearts to be able to overflow infinitely toward You.  
In such a heart, please place the creation ideology  
with which You created all things,  
so that when You move, our hearts may move,  
and when You settle, our hearts may be able to settle.  
Beloved Father, You who desired to see  
the quiet heart and enjoy the sight of it,  
now may our hearts and our feelings be moved by You  
and be used only for You.  
Thus, may our bodies and hearts  
be able to be filled only with Yours,  
and may we be able to dwell in the world of essence.  
I earnestly hope and wish for this.  
Though there are countless people living on the earth,  
there are no groups struggling to hide and bury  
their heart foundation and feelings in You.  
Today, our hearts long for the original heart,  
and the nature of original creation is required.  
For this, we know that Your new word is necessary.  
Even though the humans You created to please You  
have fallen and live in an evil world,  
they are still moving toward the world of original nature.  
For 6,000 years, they have awaited the words of original recreation  
to awaken their nature,  
and for 6,000 years, they have longed for and sought such words.

that is struggling in the world of fear,  
this humanity that wanders without knowing where to go,  
this humanity that has lost its center  
and does not know where to stand or find a place to rest.  
Please guide them back to Your embrace.
The children gathered here know that this is a sanctuary where our Father can visit and is an essential foundation. If our Father does not operate, all creations on this earth will face a day of judgment and suffer endless pain, so, Father, please extend Your hand of re-creation. 

Is there not the original principle of creation that created Adam and Eve to love? Based on that principle, in order to restore humanity before You, allow me to understand the heart of the Father who holds me, regardless of fatigue, injustice, sorrow, resentment, and tears, and even the altar of blood. Please guide me to understand the historical circumstances of the Father that cannot be helped. Understanding the Father's urgent heart, let this time be filled only with what belongs to the Father, and remove everything else. If the Father rejoices, we can also rejoice, and if the Father is moved, allow us to be moved as well. Thus, let us appear before all creation in our original form, adorned with the glory of beauty, and restore us to be able to spread a new voice. Beloved Father, I earnestly hope and desire for this.

I have realized that this mind is not my own, and that this body is not my own, and I have come to know that the land I live on is not mine. I have come to understand that this universe is not mine, and that all created things are not mine. Everything originates from the Father and is connected to the Father's will, created for the Father. 

Knowing that all people should seek the glory of joy regarding this one center that has been created is the nature of creation. Please restore us to the essence of that harmony, where our hearts can resonate with the glory of the established center, and the entire universe can resonate together.

Now the time has come when we must settle the history of cosmic sorrow and create a new history of joy. Father, we are lacking in strength, so please grant us strong power and allow us to have strong desires. Grant us the appearance of heavenly soldiers equipped with new bravery, so that we can confidently advance toward our goals, Father, I earnestly hope for this.

To Joshua and Caleb looking at the land of Canaan, You said, "Be strong and courageous." The standard set before Joshua facing the enemy was to be strong and courageous, so today we too must advance boldly toward the city of Canaan. 

At this time, when the final battle is at hand, we know that sons and daughters who can take responsibility and fight against the forces of darkness on this earth are needed. Father, please allow Your sons and daughters gathered here to become such responsible individuals. Beloved Father, I earnestly hope and desire for this.

Please govern the hearts of the sons and daughters gathered here. Is there anyone who asserts themselves today? Is there anyone who approaches the Father through their own ideas, thoughts, or perceptions? Such a person does not understand the Father's absolute authority and does not know the pain behind the Father.

Father, please hold our hearts so that we can hear the new words of life from the Father and through new feelings of love, allow us to raise the history of re-creation. 

Let us realize our shortcomings and immaturity, and allow us to be sons and daughters who can bow our heads, acknowledging that we are incomplete. Father, I earnestly hope and desire for this. 

The nature moves toward one ideal, so may our bodies and minds also move according to that will. At this time, allow our hearts and bodies to become one, and let this unified body and heart be offered as a sacrifice. 

Please allow us to break through the barriers of death that have been blocked for six thousand years with resentment and sorrow. So that countless saints can resonate, and many spirits in the spiritual world centered on the Triune God can sing songs of joy at this time. Please allow this hour to be one where we can promise the day of return and reconciliation before all beings, Father, I earnestly hope and desire for this.

I earnestly hope and desire that this time will be one where the heart leads and gathers the whole world into one before the Father's altar. 

Now, as I wish to convey the words, please allow the heart of the speaker and the heart of the listener not to become two. If the words are to move the heart, please allow us to feel with our hearts, and let us be led to the appearance of the Father's substance through our bodies. 

May Satan not find any opportunity, and please separate the elements that Satan can accuse. Father, please personally operate. 

If we do not realize our own shortcomings, please manifest with fiery eyes, and claim our bodies and hearts as Yours, and come upon us. Please allow us to be those who can fulfill the mission of indemnity and restoration through the conditions of suffering, and raise that history. 

I offer all these words in Your name. Amen. 

<Words> The title I wish to briefly speak to you about today is "Humanity Wandering in Search of Truth." I will speak with this title in mind. 

The necessity of the reality of humanity and the standard of absolute goodness. Today, you are well aware that you feel an indescribable urgency and a sense of sadness. However, within my body, there is a heart, and within that heart, there is a desire for a certain purpose, and there is a movement of power that seeks to infinitely absorb my body into the essence of that purpose, which you cannot deny. 

You cannot deny that you are in a living condition that seems to lead you in some aimless direction. If you feel this way, you must return to yourself and reassess your body and heart. Furthermore, if there is some ideological, formless world that humanity today does not know, you must reassess yourself centered on the spirit of that spiritual world. 

Thus, you must find a self that can move toward one direction, forming an integral relationship with that spirit, not as two separate entities, but as one. If you do not do this, there can be no peace in your heart, and even if you seek happiness and something else, that desire will not be fulfilled. This is what I assert to you first. 

As you have learned through principles, humanity was originally a good being. However, history proves that this good humanity became an unworthy existence due to a single mistake, and our religious beliefs also testify to this. I cannot deny that fact either. 

The standard of goodness is the standard of life and the standard of the ideals pursued by the whole. It is the center of eternal love that moves within our hearts and the focal point of emotional ideals. It leads my heart to seek some absolute resting place today. It also acts as a force that regulates my body, directs my heart, and restrains the ideals that I aim for, transcending time and space. 

Today, when viewed from my own center, whether centered on the body, heart, or spirit, each must become one center. So how can humanity today find the lost self? We must recall the heart of God at the time of loss. Without doing so, there is no way to find the original self. Without presenting such a movement, humanity cannot find the original self.

He has fought to find humanity with the heart of that time, which has been lost for six thousand years. You must understand this heart of God. 

Because the sorrow began from God's heart six thousand years ago, the history until today has remained a history of sorrow, and we have borne the fruit of sorrow. that you must understand the fact that God sheds tears and guides us through His providence.

So, what has humanity lost due to the fall? It has lost love. The reason humanity groans is that it has lost God's love. Thus, the history of humanity has also passed through a path of groaning while losing God's love. Do you understand?

God's love is the foundation of the eternal ideal of the heavenly kingdom that can build the substantial world of the kingdom on earth. Consequently, God's love, which can establish the kingdom on earth, has been gradually collapsing.

The model and path of the fall of humanity, which became the prototype of historical development, has been described as the loss of God's love. When we consider the historical path of that fall, what path did it take? Initially, Eve lost God's love. Then Adam did, and subsequently, their children did as well. You are likely aware of this. This is the path of the fall, which means that the history of humanity has also been a history of losing love.

So, who was the first to discuss love? It was Eve in the Garden of Eden. Who came next? It was Adam. Then came Cain and Abel. This is the prototype of the fallen history that humanity's lineage has walked before heaven. Because this model of the fall occurred at the beginning of human history, humans have continued to go through this history until now.

Therefore, love is the center that can govern the universe. It is the subjective center, the governing center, and the tolerant center. This is the ideal of love, and this ideal has become the foundation of history.

Thus, when we examine the historical path, we see that in primitive times, there was a matriarchal clan society. This is because Eve, the mother, was the first to discuss love. As this progressed through tribal societies, it transitioned to a patriarchal-centered history. Then, in today's democratic age, it has become a brotherhood-centered era.

This historical descent has now reached its end. Today, we can no longer find love for parents among humanity. This is the case in today's democratic nations.

Eventually, there will come a time when even the concept of marriage from the perspective of brotherhood will be broken. Thus, today, the ladder of love through which heaven can connect with humanity is being severed. Therefore, today, humanity lives like orphans who have lost parental love, true marital love, and true brotherly love.

Until now, in advanced nations, this has unfolded vertically, but currently, these issues are occurring globally and horizontally.

So, how did the fall occur? Adam and Eve could not establish a vertical relationship with God and instead formed a relative and horizontal relationship with Satan, which led to the fall. Therefore, in today's historical end times, democracy is centered around advocating for equality.

What happened in Adam's family due to the fall? Cain killed Abel. Abel represents the substitute existence of Eve. Therefore, in today's advanced nations, while advocating for equality, women hold more authority than men. Thus, this is a time when we must establish a vertical aspect through the horizontal aspect. However, because a complete vertical relationship has not been established, we see the global situation breaking apart.

(Matthew 10:37). On the surface, where is there such contradictory and nonsensical talk?
