Fallen humans are beings who have lost love. Jesus came to restore heavenly love on earth as the protagonist of love, but he could not do so and went to the spirit world. Thus, humanity is walking the path of establishing a spiritual standard of love while restoring physical love. You must understand this.

Human beings have above and below, front and back, left and right. The one above represents parents, the one below represents children, the front and back represent couples, and the left and right represent siblings. This is the principle of love. Do you understand?

Humanity must find this path, and among them, the relationship between husband and wife, which is a front-and-back relationship, is the most important. That is why Jesus emphasized the bride and groom the most.

So what kind of heart does Jesus have when seeking the bride? He seeks a bride who represents God, a bride who represents children, and a bride who represents siblings. Do you understand? God's will is to send the bride and groom to establish a standard on earth. That will is to have God above, children below, and siblings on the left and right, forming a shape of mutual expectation. The history of seeking such a bride, who represents that love, is the providential path of 2,000 years.

Now, what must you do? A man must respect women, and a woman must respect men. Only with a heart of mutual respect can a woman face a man and a man face a woman. A man is the embodiment of the father, and a woman is the embodiment of the mother. They are the incarnations.

Therefore, in the process of restoration today, when men and women face each other, those who follow each other based on appearances will break apart. One must think of the other as the one essence of God's duality and respect them as a man if they are a woman, and as a woman if they are a man.

With a heart of mutual respect, you must seek the relative qualities of each individual. This is the path that original humans must walk. Even when dealing with children, no matter how much they are your own, you must think of them as the embodiment of the father's spirit and the embodiment of the mother's spirit, and have a heart that respects that essence. Moreover, you must become parents who can embrace and love their children with the ideal of God, who created all things and summed them up, creating humanity as the protagonists of all things. While looking at those children in the fallen world, you must become true parents who can shed tears, saying, "You are the original person whom God rejoices in, whom humanity longs for, and whom all things await."

From this perspective, Jesus has qualified to face all things and the universe. Therefore, Jesus sought the bride with the feeling that she is the representative of God, the representative of humanity, and the representative existence of future generations. You must understand that this was the heart of Jesus as the bridegroom. On the day he finds such a bride, you will feel the love that embraces Heaven and Earth. The same goes for parents and children. You must become the protagonists of such love.

The day must come when the bride and groom, who can replace parents and children, meet with the feelings of the ideal of oneness and have the substantial form.
I will do it. Only when that day comes can all the tragic aspects of the universe, that is, the created world, or everything that has been blocked in heaven and earth, move harmoniously in all directions. You must understand that this day is the day humanity has been longing for.

The ideal garden where humans and God can become one
So, where should humanity today seek to go? We must seek this one place. To find this one place, you must have that heart towards your parents, that heart towards your siblings, and that heart towards your partner. You must be able to feel the emotion that represents the world through that one heart.

You must have such a heart of love to stand before heaven and earth. Only then can God, who has worked for 4,000 years to establish Jesus and the Holy Spirit, bring together the substantial bridegroom and the substantial bride. Establishing such a relationship is God's purpose of creation, and finding such a substantial counterpart is the goal humanity is walking towards. Then, the ideal garden where God can enter into the human body and become one will unfold. You must understand that this is the ultimate goal humanity is seeking and the inevitable standard point of destiny that humanity must find. Let us pray.

<Prayer> Father, I have come to realize that my individual self is a substitute for God, a substitute for a couple, a substitute for parents, a substitute for children, and a substitute for siblings in front of humanity that is searching for the truth. We also understand that there is an inevitable historical process that must be accomplished in the universe through my individual self, which can determine the position of such a great fundamental existence.

Now, within my individual self, the man is seeking a true older sister, a true younger sister, a true mother, and a true partner, and I also know that the woman is seeking a true partner. This is humanity that is searching for the same ideology, humanity that is in the same position, humanity that cannot become enemies, and humanity that must be intertwined with the creation ideology.

However, due to the fall of humanity, the love of parents has been broken, the love of couples has been broken, and the love of siblings has been broken. Therefore, in order for us to seek this today, we must first feel the emotion of love between brothers and brothers. Furthermore, we have come to understand that in order to restore the principled standard that can substitute for heaven and earth, we must find a counterpart that can love in place of God's 6,000 years of sorrow.

Today, our one form is not a simple existence but a being that must have four-dimensionality (四方性), which means that if we do not have brothers, it is sad; if we do not have friends, it is sad; if we do not have parents, it is sad; and if we do not have children, it is sad. This is because humanity, which has four-dimensionality, is searching for the truth, and loving one another is the universal principle, which is the first standard of life granted by God. Therefore, when we encounter such phenomena in our current lives, we become sad, and I earnestly wish and hope that the sons and daughters gathered here will come to understand this.

Now, grant us the heart that can embrace humanity in place of God, the heart that can embrace the Son, and the heart that can embrace the Holy Spirit. Allow us to be able to embrace the children of heaven and think of heaven and earth with such a heart. I earnestly ask and hope that a day may come when we can meet joyfully, even while being sad and suffering, and return to the center of the eternal world of all things.

Father, those who do not have a brother to love at the terminus of the journey searching for the truth will be judged; those who do not have beloved children will be persecuted; and those who do not have beloved parents, and those who do not meet beloved bride and bridegroom will be judged. Please allow us to understand this.

According to this absolute principle, from my body, the parents of the body, the siblings of the body, the spouse of the body, from my heart, the parents of the heart, the siblings of the heart, the spouse of the heart, and in the eternal ideological world, centered on the spirit, the parents of the spirit, the siblings of the spirit, and the spouse of the spirit must be established. Please allow us to achieve the three-dimensional form of the three parents, three siblings, and three spouses in the flat plane of my individual self. We must meet a day when we can be recognized by God as a substantial fruit and be blessed. Without this, we cannot solve all our problems today.

Now I must search for the true parents of my physical body, the true parents of my heart, and the true parents of my spirit, where the parents of the spirit are You, Father, the parents of the heart are the returning Lord, and the parents of the body are my biological parents. I earnestly hope that You will allow me to find my corresponding children, siblings, and partners.

I pray in Your name. Amen. 

4)
The Sorrowful Heart of Heaven
Matthew 1:18-2:12
<Prayer (I)> We know the historical facts that have left behind unspeakable tragedies and sorrows, and we understand that the heart of the Father, who rejoiced while looking at the Garden of Eden, turned into a heart of sorrow due to the fall of Adam and Eve, and that this became a historical sorrow over the long period of 6,000 years. We also know that we bear the historical responsibility to restore the lost Garden of Eden by holding onto the heart of the Father who is concerned with all our hearts and bodies.

Father! We understand that after 4,000 years of effort to find the lost Adam and Eve, the one who was sent to this earth with the form of Adam was Jesus. The greater the effort of the Father until the birth of Jesus, the more the appearance of Jesus, born from that effort, should have become a source of pride for heaven and a pride for all creation and humanity. Although heaven knew this fact, the earth was ignorant and did not know, and while heaven welcomed this, the earth did not know and could not welcome it. We cannot help but feel ashamed of this today.

Recalling the pitiful fact that the Father's hopeful gaze had to rest on the miserable appearance of Jesus lying in the manger, we deeply feel the disbelief and unfaithfulness of our ancestors. We know that humanity has once again manifested the faults of the fall of Adam and Eve. Today, we can only feel the historical sorrow in our hearts and must be deeply saddened.

We earnestly hope and wish that we can comfort the sorrow of the Father on behalf of the Israelite people, who could not comfort the Father in the past, the chosen people. Although it has been 2,000 years since Jesus came and went, we know that the world of the heart transcends time. Father, who exists beyond history, allow us to comfort the heart of Jesus Christ, who went to heaven with a sorrowful heart.

We recognize the deep resentment that remains in heaven and earth until this time, the sorrow of 2,000 years since Jesus came and went, and we earnestly hope and wish that we can receive the appearance of Jesus at the time of His birth in our hearts.

Father, bless this hour that commemorates that day, and may the joy and glory that Jesus wished for be manifested so that the sorrow that Jesus felt 2,000 years ago may be resolved through this day. We, who know all the inner feelings, wish to commemorate this day, so please allow us to be able to indemnify all the past sorrows that humanity has left behind through this hour, and allow us to stand before You, so that Jesus may rejoice and the Father may be comforted.

We are those who bear the overall mission of restoration and are in the position of having to find the one parent of restoration. You know that we are in the position of having to welcome Jesus as our true older brother. Please allow us to be able to comfort the sorrowful facts left on this earth from the standpoint of being true siblings.

There are many people on this earth searching for a way to live toward heaven, but they do not know the meaning of the power of Your life. Father! Please directly govern their hearts and bodies during this hour. Mobilize all spiritual movements so that they may understand Your overall will that announces the end days, and allow them to grasp Your inner heart. Thus, we earnestly hope and wish that the day of joy when Your true sons and daughters can become true will soon come upon this earth.

We know that Jesus, who walked the path of suffering on the cross, is cooperating with such matters, so please encourage us, who are on the earth, to fulfill Your will with all our heart and strength, and allow the brothers on this earth to unite and move forward.

Please allow this offering of our hearts, bound together and dedicated to You, to become a historical offering of indemnity, and may this holy time allow us to find the origin of happiness through indemnifying the long-standing resentment left behind.

Father, this is a brief act of worship, but please bless it, and with our insufficient hearts and bodies, please govern according to Your will. We earnestly ask that only the glory of the grace that can manifest may appear here. In the name of the Lord, we pray. Amen.

<Prayer (II)> Father, please again grant Your blessing over all people at this time. Please extend Your hand of blessing over the thirty million people of this nation at this time. Grant the gift of love to the countless children who remember Your name, and especially bless the heads of those children who have bowed down to pray in this lonely place. 

There are family members who are worried about You at this time, wanting to comfort the sorrows left on the land where sin remains, so please remember this and bless us at this time.

All people on this earth do not know this day, do not realize the sorrows of heaven that have been bound, and do not understand Your endlessly sorrowful heart even more. For us, who do not know the lamentable facts of that day, Father, please allow this day so that all people can celebrate this day as the birth of Christ, and we cannot help but thank You for granting us the grace of glory.

Please allow this day of celebration to be an opportunity to comfort the heart of Jesus, who has been sorrowful for 2,000 years. As we recall the one who was born in a sorrowful place and devoted over thirty years of life without caring about the path to Golgotha, may this hour allow us to inherit His achievements as our legacy. We know that this time must be a time when we can receive the mission left by Him.

Father! The resentment left by Jesus still remains on this earth, but the people on this earth do not know it. Now, allow the sons and daughters gathered here to have their bodies and hearts deeply moved by Your heart and to be caught in Your heart, so that they may know the heart of the young Jesus and realize the heart of Jesus, who was in a state of death, and be able to comfort Him.

Although humanity does not know, may this time allow us to realize that Jesus has been working in the spirit world until now. Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. In this hour, with our insufficient bodies and hearts, we bow before You to celebrate this day, so please come and allow us to pioneer a new ideology of restoration, and we earnestly hope and wish that overflowing grace may be manifested here. Father, remember this day and bless this day.

Now, I would like to share a message for a brief moment, so I earnestly ask for Your presence. Please allow all that we pray and ask for on this day to remain as conditions for indemnifying what has been bound in heaven and on earth.

This precious day is an important day when we must leave a mark of victory before You, even if we take up a new purpose. Please remember this day. When we earnestly ask for You to manifest with joy, we pray in the name of the Lord. Amen.

<Words> Today may be an important day that God has hoped for. It is also a day I have hoped for as I come out to fulfill the purpose. And at the same time as indemnifying through the four numbers, this time of finding the new three numbers and indemnifying is truly a time of historical connection that you must first remember.

So, the title of the message I would like to briefly share with you is "The Sorrowful Heart of Heaven." I would like to commemorate this day with this message.

The Sorrow of God Bound by Humanity
God created all things to make one person. From the first day to the fifth day, when He looked at the created things, He rejoiced with infinite hope and joy.

Thus, as the main character of all these creations, God created our ancestors, Adam and Eve, as the masters who govern all things in place of God. And He blessed them with an infinitely joyful heart. That is, He told them to be fruitful and multiply and fill the earth. (Genesis 1:28) The blessing of being fruitful and multiplying and filling the earth was given to us humans to please God, meaning that humanity was created for this purpose. God also blessed us to fulfill this purpose.

However, Adam and Eve could not fulfill that blessing. Thus, the sorrowful history has flowed until this time without that blessing being fulfilled, and you must recall this fact once again during this hour.

When Adam was growing, heaven was infinitely joyful. All creation was giving joy to heaven through Adam. However, because Adam, who did not fully understand the heavenly will, could not uphold the will and words of heaven, he became bound by the sorrowful yoke of the fall.

God, who established the laws of heaven and earth and the heavenly principles, had to cast Adam and Eve out of His loving embrace due to their fall. All of creation knew of God's sorrowful heart, and the good spirits of the angelic world knew it, but we, the descendants of fallen humanity, have not known it until now. You all must be well aware of this fact today.

We have gathered to commemorate this day. We have gathered to celebrate the birth of Jesus. So, who was Jesus? He was the one who lost...
He was the being that Heaven found and established in place of the fallen Adam. Therefore, at that time, people should have been able to hold the baby Jesus and weep on behalf of God, feeling the sorrow that had been lodged in God's heart for 4,000 years since the birth of Jesus, and they should have been able to hold the baby Jesus and rejoice on His behalf. There should have been many such people, yet there was not a single person who could hold the newborn Jesus and rejoice, nor anyone who could hold Him and weep on behalf of God.

God's sorrow is rooted in humanity, and God's sorrow cannot be resolved by God alone. For the deep sorrow lodged in God's heart to be released, it must be through people. Because this sorrow is bound to humanity, if people cannot weep on behalf of God, the sorrow lodged within God cannot be resolved. You must understand this fact.

Even though Mary and Joseph were in a position to look at the baby Jesus lying in the manger and weep on behalf of God, they did not know that God's inner heart was so sorrowful. Therefore, we must recognize that Joseph and Mary, even while looking at Jesus in the manger, could not truly weep for Heaven.

And the three wise men from the East, the shepherds, and Anna, among others, had hearts that bore witness to Jesus and rejoiced. However, there was not a single person who understood that before they could rejoice, there was sorrow lodged in God's heart.

So what should we do now? We must be able to feel the sorrow of God for having lost Adam and at the same time rejoice in the fact that Jesus was born. To release the sorrow deeply lodged in God's heart, we must restore this world of sin that was brought about by our human ancestors. To restore this sinful world, we must have a heartfelt desire to weep on behalf of God and become individuals who can hold Jesus and weep. If Joseph and Mary had become such people, they would have upheld the will of Jesus. Likewise, if the wise men had such hearts, they too would have followed the will of Jesus.

The sorrow of God that no one knew and the hope of Mary and Joseph

However, Joseph and Mary, who worked for Jesus and upheld His will, could not truly face Jesus with the sorrowful heart of Heaven, nor could the three wise men look at Jesus as Heaven looked upon Him with sorrow.

Today, we must first recall the heart of God who was sorrowful until Jesus was born. We must remember the sorrowful heart of God when He expelled Adam and Eve from the Garden of Eden, and the heartbreaking scene of God watching the only begotten Adam being led away by the enemy Satan. You must recall this in your heart.

To resolve this sorrow, God sent numerous prophets over the course of 4,000 years after the fall of Adam and Eve to inform humanity of this sorrowful situation. However, because humans did not understand this sorrow of God and did not recognize the sorrow of the prophets sent by Heaven, the people of Israel went through a history of betraying Heaven. God worked tirelessly, not resting for a moment, to fulfill His will. Ultimately, after 4,000 years of history, He was finally able to restore the lost Adam, and it was then that Mary and Joseph appeared.

So what position were Joseph and Mary in? Adam and Eve fell at the stage of engagement, and Joseph and Mary were in the same position. God placed Joseph and Mary in such a position and guided them. It took 4,000 years to choose and establish such Joseph and Mary. You must understand this.

When we consider the motivations that brought Mary and Joseph before God, Mary, though young, understood that God was working through this nation. And Mary earnestly hoped for the Messiah to come to this earth more than anyone else. Joseph also earnestly hoped for the Messiah who could save his people and lead the chosen Israelites into the kingdom of Heaven.

Mary and Joseph longed for the Messiah to come with all their hearts and were confident that God's will would be fulfilled. They believed that if they devoted themselves sincerely, the Messiah would surely be born in some way, and they hoped for the announcement of that birth with their sincere devotion. We must understand this.

In the past, Adam and Eve fell due to disbelief, but they had a heart of faith representing their nation, a heart longing for the Messiah to come, a heart of sincere devotion, and a heart of loyalty. This heart moved God and became the motivation for God to promise to send the Messiah to Israel.

When the angel appeared to Mary to announce that she would conceive the Messiah, Mary was taken aback. She denied that such a thing could happen because she had not known a man. However, with a sincere heart towards her father's will, Mary responded to the angel's command, saying, "I am the Lord's servant; may it be to me as you have said." Yet this response was contrary to the law of Israel that the Jewish people had upheld for 4,000 years. Because a virgin conceiving was an impossible event, the law of Moses was so strict that a virgin who became pregnant would be stoned to death immediately. Nevertheless, Mary made this decision.

Thus, as a virgin, especially as an engaged virgin, Mary was placed in a position where she had to resolve the issue of life or death before Heaven. She was also in a significant position that could impact her relatives and society as a whole.

Mary's great determination to conceive the Messiah

However, Mary resolved that she could give up everything in this world, but she could not give up her father's will, and she was determined to accept any hardship in order to fulfill her father's will. At that moment, when Mary offered up all her dignity, reputation, her entire life, and even her life itself as a sacrifice on behalf of all humanity, the connection for the Messiah to be born was finally established.

Moreover, we must understand the situation of Mary, who conceived the Messiah and was entrusted with a body before Heaven, and who had to infinitely worry about the path she would take after the birth of the Messiah. Her situation mirrored God's own difficult circumstances, and her worries reflected God's heart that was concerned for the evil world. Thus, God commanded the angel to instruct Joseph to protect Mary.

Joseph also heard from the angel that Mary, to whom he was engaged, had conceived, but from a human perspective, this was a difficult situation to accept. However, knowing that God establishes humans to fulfill His great purpose and works through them, Joseph welcomed Mary according to the angel's command.

We must think that the cooperation of Mary and Joseph became the foundation for restoring the lost Adam from Eden. Today, if you were to return to the time of Jesus 2,000 years ago and find yourselves in the position of Mary and Joseph, what would you do? If Heaven came to you with earnest circumstances and desired to establish a connection with you, what attitude would you take? What heart would you have when facing Heaven?

If you cannot appear before Heaven with the heart of Mary or Joseph, then your position today, celebrating the Jesus born, who was born through the heart of Mary and Joseph, cannot be considered a suitable position before Heaven.

Therefore, you must reflect on whether you are truly in the position of Joseph or Mary. Whenever Heaven commands you, you must follow that will and believe in it, even if it means denying all social customs, traditions, and ethical views you have believed in and followed, just like Joseph and Mary did. Thus, you must stand in a position where you can celebrate the birth of Jesus with faith that is willing to risk your life to overcome these issues.

God, after sending Jesus, had worries that Joseph and Mary could not comprehend, and He thought of things that Joseph and Mary did not. God wished for Joseph and Mary to embrace, protect, and nurture the born Jesus with all their hearts until He would step forth as the leader of the battle against the world of enemies. He desired that they would nurture Him with all their intellect and be a living sacrifice for Jesus.

However, until Jesus was born, Joseph and Mary were united in having a heart that worried about God's desires, but after Jesus was born, they could not share the same heart as God and looked at Jesus through the lens of their own worries and conditions, nurturing Him based on their own living conditions.

Joseph and Mary were to be the protectors of Jesus, the fence around Him, and the shield in His battles. Therefore, they had to uphold Jesus, who appeared on behalf of God's heart, whether in life or death. They were to risk their lives for God and uphold Jesus. The growing Jesus was their son, yet He was not a son belonging to them.

The sorrow of Jesus who was not treated as the Messiah

If Joseph and Mary had maintained the determination they had when conceiving Jesus throughout His growth, they could have prevented the path of the cross for Jesus.

We know that Jesus left His family to seek disciples because the internal and external circumstances that the parents should have cooperated in were not fulfilled.

That is why, at the wedding feast in Cana of Galilee, when Mary asked Jesus to turn water into wine, He said to her, "Woman, why do you involve me?" (John 2:4). When we think of this statement, we can see that Mary did not understand the thoughts Jesus held in His heart. Joseph did not understand, nor did His beloved brothers. Jesus was concerned for Heaven with His heart, and He was concerned for His living environment with His body. While it was natural for Jesus to be concerned for God, it was a sorrowful fact that He had to worry about His living environment.

Jesus was born sorrowfully and grew up sorrowfully. He, who should have lived only for God and worried only about God, lost His living environment and was placed in a position where He had to worry about God with His heart and about His livelihood with His body. We must understand this sad fact.

Thus, Jesus leaving His family meant leaving His brothers, and it meant leaving the lineage of Joseph that had passed for 4,000 years. When Jesus looked at all the crowds who did not believe in Him, His heart was filled with a sorrow that could not be expressed to anyone.

The pain in Jesus's heart was not because His circumstances were sorrowful and difficult, but because His mother, brothers, and relatives did not recognize Him. This single fact became the greatest sorrow for Jesus.

Therefore, today we must restore the original position of Mary, the position of Joseph, the position of Jesus's brothers, the position of Jesus's lineage, and further, we must restore the position of Jesus Himself. We must understand that there are historical grievances that must not be left unresolved.

Then, you must deeply feel the life of Jesus, who was born, lived for about 30 years, and carried the cross, and you must keenly feel the sorrow that Jesus experienced, whether in heart or body. You must not only celebrate the birth of Jesus. Only by understanding the Jesus who was born and then sorrowfully left can you qualify to celebrate the birth of Jesus.

The scene of Joseph and Mary looking upon the born Jesus may have been a condition of joy before God, but because they could not embrace and celebrate the entirety of Jesus's life, they left behind the result of not establishing a condition of joy before God.

When we think of this, we must welcome the born Jesus while also recognizing the Jesus who left. Thus, we must have the heart to celebrate the born Jesus while following the Jesus who went to the cross. We must understand that this is the Jesus who fought in such a way, and we must know all the feelings He experienced in His life and inherit those feelings in our dealings with Him; otherwise, we will not have the qualification to celebrate the Jesus who came and went.

Therefore, today we must regard the sorrow of Jesus as our own true sorrow and the suffering of Jesus's life as our own true suffering, and we must be able to hold the entirety of the will that Jesus has worked for over the past 2,000 years in our hearts. Only by understanding the heart of Jesus as He grew and the heart of Jesus as He suffered and went to the cross can we celebrate the Jesus who came and went, establish a connection with Him, and through Him, establish a connection with God.

The desire of Jesus for humanity

Today, we must also stand in for the wise men who came to Jesus. We must be able to prepare gifts like the three wise men who brought gold, frankincense, and myrrh and worshipped Him. We should at least have the preparations that the shepherds had when they came to worship. Just as the countless saints in Heaven rejoiced and sang when Jesus was born on earth, we must think about the fact that all creation responded to the one born Messiah, even though humanity did not know, and we must have the heart to celebrate Jesus on behalf of the whole.

We must have the heart to celebrate Jesus on behalf of the three wise men, on behalf of the shepherds, and on behalf of all creation; we must directly face Jesus with such hearts.

When that happens, the entire universe will shed endless tears. After shedding tears, we will be able to celebrate with joy. We must understand that this is the mission of humanity today after sending Jesus.

What kind of heart does Jesus wish for you to have? What heart does Jesus wish for you to commemorate this day with? If there is something that Jesus requires of us with His heart, it is to recognize the feelings He had when no one acknowledged Him during His 30 years on earth, and to understand the heart He bore while sending countless saints to their deaths throughout the 2,000 years of history. We must understand this.

Furthermore, we must also understand that Jesus hopes for us to compensate and restore the responsibilities He could not fulfill on earth on behalf of Heaven.
Now our hearts must hold onto the red heart of Jesus, and our bodies must grasp the reality of Jesus who bled, shedding tears for all people and praying for enemies. We must find the heart of Jesus, who wept for heaven and earth, and feel pain in our hearts and fatigue in our bodies.

98   The Sorrowful Heart of Heaven
With such a heart, may the sorrow of heaven be resolved through us at this time, and may the historical sorrow of Jesus be resolved through us. Only when a heart that can say this arises from your depths will God come to us and establish a connection with us. 

Although Jesus paved the way for spiritual salvation after His crucifixion, it was not a smooth path. He forged this path through the lonely road of death. Because of this Jesus, we must understand that even to this day, He is tirelessly wiping away the history of tears without a moment's rest.

Therefore, we must now hold onto Jesus, knowing that we are in a shared destiny where we must die together if He dies and live together if He lives. We must feel that Jesus' death is my death, Jesus' sorrow is my sorrow, and Jesus' anger and injustice are my anger and injustice. The deep resentment and unjust feelings that pierce Jesus' bones still remain on this earth, and we must not forget that the one who must resolve this resentment is not Jesus Himself, nor God, but us today.

If you have a heart to celebrate Jesus with a sense of joy, then you must advance toward the city of resentment that Jesus left behind, toward the land of resentment. You must fight and take responsibility first, and only then can you celebrate Jesus, understanding that He can only meet us under those conditions.

The purpose that Jesus came to fulfill on this earth has not been realized as intended, and that purpose remains as a purpose to be fulfilled even after 2,000 years of history, passed down to countless descendants.

We must become the embodiment of Jesus' purpose. The purpose left by Jesus is one that must be fulfilled even while dying on the cross, a purpose that must be fulfilled even if it stands in a place where God does not know it, and a purpose that cannot be abandoned even if the nation betrays Him or if some close person on this land betrays Him. You must stand in a position where you declare that you will fulfill that purpose.

In embracing this purpose, no matter what betrays you or what obstructs you, you must stand firm in the position that I have taken on the purpose left by Jesus and fight for it as a matter of course. If you cannot do this, you must understand that you cannot fulfill the purpose left by Jesus, nor can you resolve the resentment He left behind.

If we do not fulfill the purpose left by Jesus and resolve the resentment He left behind, we cannot resolve the will and resentment of God, who has sought us for 2,000 years.

Thus, we are
today's individuals, but we must know that we are not just individuals. We are individuals connected to the entire universe, hoping to represent the heart of historical entirety, hoping to represent the whole purpose of Jesus, and further, recognizing that God's heart remains to entrust us with responsibilities for the future.

You must realize that you are in such a historically significant position and be able to call upon Jesus and God. The heart of God, which has been longing for 4,000 years, and the heart of Joseph and Mary, through which Jesus was born, have a fervent desire that has been looking upon us as He lived for over 30 years, and we must understand that this is urgently required of us today.

Do you have a heart that reaches out to heaven, raising your hands in hope of salvation? Do you have a heart that bends down in repentance toward heaven? Do you have a heart that can move your limbs and run toward heaven? Do you have the heart to take responsibility for the majestic struggle of Jesus, who fought before the cross, with all your readiness of heart and body? You must again realize that if you do not take responsibility for the movement to resolve the historical resentment left behind, you will not be able to fulfill your mission.

Then what will Jesus announce to us today? Jesus came to this earth seeking true sons and daughters who could genuinely express His heart and convey the circumstances of heaven, yet He could not find true sons and daughters. For over 30 years, He struggled to find someone with whom He could share life and death, someone who could inherit the heavenly legacy, but He could not meet such a person and left without being able to pass it on.

Understanding this heart of Jesus, you must also bear the same responsibility and stand in the same position to call upon heaven as Father, to look upon all people on earth and cry out in repentance, and to call upon all creation to bless heaven with a heartfelt cry. If you do not have such emotional impulses, you must reflect on the fact that you cannot face the countless prophets and sages who have fought through the ages and have come through the place of death, honoring the Jesus who has come and the Jesus who has left, and who is still suffering.

Now we must raise our hands in supplication before the Father. 
Father! At this time, we earnestly ask that you allow us to take the place of the body of Jesus who came to this earth 2,000 years ago. We must plead that this body, placed before your altar, be allowed to represent the Jesus who came and went 2,000 years ago.

Now we must place our hearts and make a vow toward heaven. Our hearts and intentions must be able to represent the heart and intention of Jesus, and our physical bodies must be able to represent the body of Jesus. We must become the embodiment of Jesus, who wished to hold heaven in heart and hold the earth and all humanity with our bodies. Thus, we must become those who can fight while holding heaven in our hearts and humanity on this earth with our bodies.

The True Wish of Jesus
What Jesus ate was not for Himself, what He lived for was not for Himself, what He grieved for was not for Himself, and what He lamented was not for Himself. Even in sorrow, Jesus looked upon the Father, who was grieving more than Himself, and felt ashamed. Even in pain, He thought that the pain of heaven was greater and bowed His head, feeling a stronger sense of responsibility as the Son of Heaven. We must emulate this image of Jesus.

Jesus, who appeared with the responsibility to save the people of disbelief, faced many paths of suffering, toil, and anguish throughout His 30 years of life, yet He did not mind. We must understand the heart of Jesus, who lamented even in dreams about the inability of the Israelite people to stand before the Father.

The more earnest our hearts are in facing the purpose, the more we must appear with a heartfelt desire to hold heaven in our hearts and the earth in our bodies. Even as He walked the path of Golgotha, even in the place where He bled, even in the place where His blood and flesh melted away, He held onto heaven and cared for all people. Today, we must understand this heart.

Jesus was a pitiful figure. He had parents but did not have true parents; He had brothers but did not have true brothers; He had disciples but did not have true disciples.

We must restore this historical reality so that we can become the true parents of Jesus, the true brothers of Jesus, the true disciples of Jesus, and we must not fail to become the true congregation of Jesus.

Younger individuals should have overflowing hearts to honor and serve the older ones as true parents. Likewise, older individuals should look upon the younger ones as if they were their own children, embracing them with all their hearts and being willing to become offerings themselves.

Jesus longed for true brothers, yet He could not fulfill that longing to approach heaven with true brothers, a longing that He held until His last breath. This was the resentment of Jesus. The providential history to restore lost love

What is it that all of humanity living on this earth is seeking today? They are seeking cosmic parents. In particular, Christian believers are hoping for the emergence of denominational parents. The day when the cosmic parent appears is the day of the Second Coming. However, the providence that can bring about the meeting of denominational parents has not yet been fulfilled. 
Heaven has been establishing the will of providence for 6,000 years, but when we see that the mission of the Second Coming, which must come centered on the denomination and take on the responsibility of the high priest, remains, we can understand that while the providence within the promise of the bride and groom has been fulfilled, the bride and groom have not yet reached the position of true parents who can live centered on the denomination. Before the position of true parents is determined, a true family composed of true children cannot be established. Furthermore, until the position of cosmic parents is determined, the position of denominational parents cannot be established. 
Today, fallen humans have parents, but those parents are not true parents. Those parents are not recognized by God. 
So, what must we, who are at the end, do? We must receive the cosmic parent, the denominational parent, and then the familial parent. In other words, we must receive the three generations of parents. 
A family is a form that can represent the people, the denomination can represent the children, and the cosmic parent can represent the true parents. 

Restoring the Nation of Victory
Today, while humans live on the earth, they are stepping outside the realm of the love of true parents permitted by heaven. This connection, which should link parents and blood and flesh from birth to the eternal world, is a sorrowful reality. 
Therefore, only when the love of God is intertwined from familial parents to denominational parents and cosmic parents can we finally enter the realm of love that encompasses the entire 6,000 years and stand before God with our faces raised. You must understand that this is the path we humans must inevitably take. 

Where we stand and what we must do
So, where do we stand now? We are still in a position where we have not yet entered the realm of familial true parents. Therefore, we must seek out the position of familial true parents, but we cannot just find those parents. Why? Because we have fallen, we must build a bridge of brotherhood to rise back up. Even if it means sacrificing everything, we must seek out true parents and establish a standard that has set the condition of historical indemnity. Otherwise, heaven cannot accept you. 
So, what must you do? Since you are in a position to receive parents, you must lay the foundation of brotherhood that can receive those parents. This is the significance of the three-stage foundation. 
When the brothers of the established three-stage foundation are equipped to receive heavenly parents and when three brothers become one and twelve brothers become one, then they can finally be granted qualification as a family of heaven. In doing so, that family must expand to represent the denomination, the nation, and the world, and must prepare a standard upon which to receive parents. 
After that, they must prepare to receive cosmic parents by establishing a denominational form. Even during Jacob's time, a familial standard was established, but because his descendants did not believe, that standard was completely broken. During Moses' time, the standard of a national family and national parents was laid down, but it was broken due to disbelief. Jesus also came to establish the standard of a global family on earth, but because humans did not believe, that will was shattered. 
Thus, today, humanity has hope and faith, but lacks love. 
Due to the fall, we have lost hope, lost faith, and lost love. Therefore, we, who are destined to seek these out again, must have new hope and new faith. Furthermore, we must establish brothers who can unite new hope and new faith into one. Thus, we must establish a standard that can represent the entire will that was sought after by hope since Jacob and by faith since Jesus. 
Only when all these substantial conditions are met can God look upon us as beings of hope and beings of faith. 
Until now, humans have looked upon God with hope and faith. However, when a substantial being with the fruits of hope and faith emerges on this earth, then God can have hope for that being. In other words, God must be able to have hope for us and we must become a substantial being that can believe, so that God's love can connect with the world. 
To achieve this, the love of parents must be established at the center of you according to the principle of indemnity and restoration, so that the love of spouses can be established. Furthermore, the love of parents and the love of spouses must be established for the love of siblings to be established. This is how it is. 
The love of parents is one. The love of spouses is for the purpose of procreation centered on parents, and the love of siblings can represent this couple for procreation. The love of parents is meant to expand from one. Fallen humanity must start from the smallest unit, which is siblings, to find this. 
If we do not start from siblings, we cannot build the ideal world. 

How to receive true parents
So, how must we receive true parents? We must become true spouses and establish a true family. Only then can we receive true parents above that. 
It is good that you believe and follow the teacher. However, you must become a being that others can believe and follow as much as you believe and follow the teacher. This is how you must establish the form of the family that Jesus sought. Only then can all people become brothers. To create this, the three-stage foundation was established. Therefore, when you do something in the future, you must not do it alone. Even in evangelism, you must not do it alone. 
When establishing this three-stage foundation, even when standing in the position of parents, you must not do it among brothers alone; you must unite with them. Only when parents and siblings unite can a family be established. And to form a national shape, this family must become twelve families. Only when there are more than ten can the conditions for a nation be represented. 
Why did Jesus establish 120 disciples? From Adam to Noah is ten generations, and from Noah to Jacob is twelve generations. The twelve sons of Jacob represent the vertical fruition that replaces all of these two thousand years, which is why Jesus centered on the number twelve. To represent the twelve generations from Noah to Jacob and the ten generations from Noah to Adam, when you descend from twelve to ten, you get 120. What does this mean? It means that it was a number representing the totality needed for restoration. That is why in the past, I often spoke about evangelizing you. 6) Humans and God Must Live Together

<Prayer (III)> Father! Please allow us to gain insight into the sorrowful heart of Jesus, who had to speak to his beloved disciples about concluding his life on earth and going to your kingdom.

<Words> The title of the message I would like to share with you today is "Humanity and God, Who Must Live Together." I will speak on this topic.

The motivation and purpose behind God creating all of creation was to live together. It is essential for everyone to understand that He created us to live together.

From the smallest to the largest, all beings that are part of the process of creation were created as joyful beings capable of moving within the realm of God's love. You all know this well.

Among them, we humans are beings that God has invested great effort into creating. We are beings of thought among thoughts, beings of heart among hearts, beings of ideals among ideals, and beings of substance among substances.

Therefore, for God to possess humanity means to possess the entire universe, and for God to govern humanity means to govern the entire created world. To rejoice with humanity means to rejoice with all of creation. You must understand that God has established humanity as a representative being that embodies the entirety of purpose from the ideal of creation to its results.

The purpose of God creating the created world is to live together, but today, humanity and all beings do not exist within the realm where they can live with God. What has caused this? We know well that it is due to the fall. Because of the fall, the foundation for God's presence has disappeared.

So, what is the reason that God has been searching for humanity from the day He lost Adam and Eve until now? It is because when we humans become the temple of God, the body of God, and a substantial being that embodies oneness with God, our joy becomes God's joy, and God's joy is connected to all creation through us. In other words, we humans are the intermediaries that connect God and all creation.

Originally, we humans should have felt that joy until today, but we have never experienced it, nor have we ever established the original temple that God intended to create, nor have we ever possessed the heart, mind, and ideals of God. This has been the reality of humanity until today.

No matter how great or admirable someone may be, if they cannot represent the ideals that God desires, they cannot be the substantial embodiment of those ideals, and they cannot possess the true form that can represent God's heart.

What has happened to humanity, who were once in that realm, who have gone through such a fate for six thousand long years?

Today, we hope to live, and tomorrow we hope to live, clinging to life with a desire for endless extension, searching for an ideal. Where is the point of hope that these humans wish to stay?

With a Creator who exists, but whom they do not recognize; with a subject of heart who exists, but whom they do not know; with the true subject of love who exists, but whom they do not recognize, humanity is searching for something else. What must God's heart be like when He sees this?

If there is no ideal of creation and no actual results of creation, that may be understandable, but if there are actual beings of creation and the ideal of creation remains within God, then a being must emerge that can complete and fulfill that ideal and those results.

But what kind of being would that be? It is neither all creation nor God; it is precisely humanity that we must come to understand. And we must realize that we must become such humanity.

That is why God has been searching for humanity for six thousand years. Until today, He has been seeking to make humanity a foundation to move toward heaven.

If humanity had not fallen, they could have completed all conditions, connected through life to the entirety of the ideal of creation, and could have become the substantial embodiment of that ideal before God. However, due to the fall, God has departed, the connections with all creation have been severed, and the connections between humans have also been cut off. This is the sorrow of sorrows, the lament of laments.

The result of the fall is not limited to my individual lament; when I look around, it is the lament of my compatriots, when I look up at the world, it is the lament of humanity, and when I look at all creation, it is the lament of all creation. When I lift my head and look at the heavenly world through my heart, it is the lament of heaven. Have you ever felt such an enormous reality?

Have you ever held that lament in your heart and body, crying out loudly? Have you ever wanted to hold onto all the lamenting creation, to be concerned about the lament of our Creator, and to hold heaven in deep sorrow, crying out for all people and all creation?

Though we may not have such hearts, if heaven searches for us with a heart of lament, you must realize that we are the most unfilial, the most treacherous, and the most betraying among all.

If there were no such heaven, that would be one thing, but if there is, we must understand that humanity living on this earth today is an unforgivable traitor.

This unfaithful humanity, this betraying humanity, this despairing humanity is still searching for conditions to be reshaped. 

Heaven is seeking to pull humanity, who are in the position of fallen Adam, to stand on the side of heaven, to complete the attributes of God's entire will from the ideal of God, and to live in consultation with them. If there is anyone who feels this, God would have no greater gratitude.

Until today, heaven has paved the way for providential management through individuals without humanity's knowledge, and you know well through the restoration process that it has paved the way for global providence through the environment.

So why has heaven fought through six thousand years of history to connect with our ancestors, our nation, and our land? What is the purpose?

God's words were not only revealed to our ancestors who betrayed them in the beginning. Throughout the six thousand years of history after the fall, God has revealed His words at any time and in any era. Knowing God's sorrowful heart in this way, and being filled with concern for God, who has worked hard for the nation for 4,000 years, he had the noble heart to pray for blessings upon his enemies by giving himself over to Satan. This is what you must understand.
Are there any Christian believers like this today? Therefore, we must share the mission given to us.
Oh God! Please give us strength. Now that we understand this, we will run toward this goal until the day our strength runs out. If we run and fall from exhaustion, please give us strength again. Only after this should we pray. When we pray, we will receive strength again. We must be prepared to run today, tomorrow, and even for 10, 20, or 40 years. Now you must seek God's word with this determination.
The nation of Israel, which betrayed Jesus who came to build the temple on this earth, could not unite with Jesus, and thus lost the reality of the temple, becoming a nation that wandered in the wilderness for 2,000 years. This is akin to betraying Moses, who was established as the leader of the nation representing heaven before the 600,000 people of Israel. The fact that the nation of Israel forsook Moses became a historical condition that allowed them to betray Jesus. Similarly, returning to the place of historical twists and turns, all of humanity today, faced with the end times, has gone through a 2,000-year process of worldwide Canaan restoration, centered on a 40-year journey for global Canaan restoration, having gone through the First and Second World Wars, and now living in the danger of a Third World War, struggling without knowing where the center of providence is.
No matter what theory or logic they rely on, they are struggling without finding a solution, and we know very well that they do not have the content and mental standards to claim that their empirical claims or ethical views are their substantial eternal standards.
This is why religion is struggling, ethics is struggling, philosophy is struggling, and all ideologies are struggling. Even scientists are struggling. This is the end times of the world, a time of tragic wilderness. It is a time when central beings cannot find the center and can betray the heavenly principles, a time when they can lose even the center they had.
The faith attitude that the saints of the end times must have
In this age, we must not become the fallen nation of Israel in the process of building global Canaan welfare, but we must equip ourselves with the ideology of the Second Israel and become figures like Joshua and Caleb, who cried out to reclaim the land of Canaan, rejecting the nation that betrayed Moses. The Bible refers to such people as the two olive trees of the end times.
Such a time will come at the end. At that time, the global Christians will struggle like the 600,000 people wandering in the wilderness. Here, we must newly recognize the ideology of the Second Chosen People and, centered on Joshua and Caleb, declare that we will march forward, shaking off all the wrong living habits of Israel until now!
Therefore, Christians today, who are faced with the end times, must move toward new Canaan welfare. We are in an urgent position where we must be armed with the ideological concepts that can lead us to new Canaan welfare. And we must become warriors who are emotionally armed to strike against the enemies that block this ideological garden. However, until now, we have been wandering vaguely in the wilderness.
Like the second generation who crossed the Jordan River and followed Joshua and Caleb to find new Canaan welfare, we must have a determination greater than when Moses came out of the palace, shaking off the cruel grasp. We must completely eliminate all the historical concepts that the past nation had and fell for. When the voice calling to eliminate such concepts is heard on the earth, believers must listen carefully and pay attention.
Now, we, the saints in the end times, must offer historical prayers toward heaven. What kind of prayer? A prayer greater than the prayer Moses offered to receive the tablets on Mount Sinai, a prayer greater than the prayer Abraham offered during the sacrifice of Isaac on Mount Moriah, a prayer greater than the prayer Jesus offered in Gethsemane, where he risked life and death, a prayer greater than the prayer he offered while carrying the cross and walking toward Golgotha, seeking God's heart step by step.
Where is the group that is filled with the heart to pray such prayers, holding onto heaven and earth with tears? You must understand that the time has come to seek this out.

Humans lamenting in ignorance

The wishes of our ancestors regarding us
