<Words> The words of the text are ones we are all too familiar with. From the first day to the sixth day, God said that all things He created were good, that is, good. We must recall once again that within this statement of goodness was the internal heart of God that He wanted to boast about infinitely. 

God Seeking Conditions for Boasting 
God looked at all the things He created over six days and wanted to boast about them. He was infinitely pleased when He looked at all creation. With that joyful heart, He repeatedly said, "It is good, it is good." To whom was this statement made? It was not to the archangel. It was a statement made to all of creation. We must understand that He spoke with such a fervent heart towards all things. 

However, all the created beings that were praised for being good in the Garden of Eden lost the value of goodness. The intention that God wanted to boast about could not be manifested in reality among all things. When we think of this sorrowful fact, we must remember once again that the statement "It is good" became a word of sadness. 

The statement "It is good" has become a word of sadness. If there had been a true original person who sincerely understood God's heart and circumstances, God would have felt even greater joy as He looked at all things created through His utmost effort. 

However, there were no offerings that understood the value standard of that statement "It is good." When we recall this, we can understand that the heart of the Father, who loved all creation, must have been filled with sorrow. Originally, God wanted to boast more about Himself, who created all things, than about the created beings that were made good. This is something we must understand. 

Therefore, the title I want to speak about today is "Let Us Know the God Who Wanted to Boast." I will speak briefly under the title "Let Us Know the God Who Wanted to Boast." 

God created Adam and Eve and desired for them to govern all things and realize the value of the word within the realm of goodness. We must once again recall the fact that God looked forward to the day when Adam and Eve could boast before all creation. 

God, looking at Adam and Eve, longed and anticipated the day when they would reach a stage of completion and govern all things, appearing as His representatives. God must have wanted to have a historical moment where He could boast about the fact that He created all things over a long period while establishing Adam and Eve. He also hoped for the day when, having established Adam and Eve, their hearts would be His heart, where if they were joyful, He would also be joyful, and if they responded, He would also respond, becoming one rather than two. We must be able to grasp this heavenly heart today. However, because our human ancestors did not understand this heart of God, they fell. We know this fact well. 

Since the beginning of creation, God has earnestly anticipated the day when a person who could be boasted about, a family that could be boasted about, would appear through human ancestors. However, due to the fall, all these conditions for boasting disappeared. The conditions for boasting turned into conditions for sorrow. As we think about this fact, we must realize that fallen humanity has a historical responsibility to delve into the heart of the Father, which is imbued with the heart of boasting, and to seek the day when we can boast before God. 

To Be a Being of Boasting Before God 
The God who created all things could not boast even for a single day or hour, and that God, whose boasting turned into sorrow and tears, is a reality we did not know. 

Therefore, this is the time for us to seek the nature that God wants to boast about and to seek the original life. Thus, you must now possess the nature of love that can face God and prepare the original form that God wanted to boast about. 

God has sought for 6,000 years for a being that can shame Satan, a being that can be boasted about, but has not found such a person up to this time. We must understand this sad reality. 

Humans love to boast. It is in human nature to want to boast about oneself. There is a desire to boast about oneself, one’s parents, siblings, and children, in other words, the entirety of one’s family. Furthermore, there is a desire to boast about one’s race, one’s country, and even the entire world and all of heaven and earth. Although fallen, the original intention to boast governs your lives and has governed history up to now. 

So, what is the reason for recognizing this desire to boast as improper today? It is because humanity has fallen. 

We want to boast about ourselves in our daily lives. We do not just want to boast to our neighbors, but to people all over the world. The desire to boast about oneself is not a bad desire; it is a desire of our original nature. This is the heart of creation that can go to the Kingdom of Heaven. 

We want to boast about ourselves, passing through family, society, nation, and reaching the world. This is the heart of those of us living on this earth. 

So, what is the reason that this desire to boast moves our hearts and stirs our emotions? It is because we have an inherent desire to boast. This desire exists because if God and humanity had achieved a unified ideal, our boasting would be God's boasting, and God's boasting would be our boasting. Therefore, even though we humans have fallen, we are still moving in this direction, and today we are struggling to find the central value of the universe. 

However, because we are fallen humans, we must understand that all the laws of boasting that move our hearts are not based on natural principles but are, on the contrary, based on contrary principles. We should have been humans who sought the laws of nature according to our original heart, but due to the fall, we lost that and must now walk the path of opposition, realizing that our original heart is in conflict with the direction and reality of our environment. 

Therefore, as we seek God and the path of virtue, we must ask ourselves whom we should boast about. Before boasting about ourselves, we must first boast about a center. If we want to boast about our country, we should establish a loyal person to boast about that country rather than boasting about ourselves. The same applies when we want to boast about a race; we should establish a center to boast about that race. The same goes for families. 

Thus, fallen humans must go beyond themselves, transcending to the center of the organization, the center of the path, the center of the nation, the center of the world, and ultimately, the center of heaven and earth, which is God, and must walk the path of boasting about that. If we do not do this, we must understand that we cannot stand before God as beings of boasting. 

To Meet the Conditions for God to Boast 
A person who boasts to make themselves happy is establishing conditions that go against the principles of heaven. Therefore, you must learn to boast about relative beings beyond your own boasting conditions. The more you can boast about the goodness of others and their characteristics, the closer you can come to heaven. 

All humans have a desire to go beyond themselves and want to boast about their families, churches, nations, and the world. However, throughout history or even today on this earth, we have not found a world, nation, church, or family that we can truly bow our heads and boast about. Humanity has not yet found a world, nation, church, or family that can be boasted about forever. 

Even though we humans stand in a position of disbelief, we must establish a connection of boasting before God. We must boast beyond ourselves about our families, societies, nations, and the world. Therefore, our hearts are always led in that direction. 

Now we must recall the heavenly heart that has been yearning to boast. When we think of the history of God's labor over 6,000 years to find us, the miserable path of struggle, we realize that at no point during that historical process did God have the conditions to boast about humanity. When we understand this divine circumstance, we realize that we cannot dare to stand before God and boast about ourselves or present any conditions. 

Originally, in the Garden of Goodness, God could boast about our individual selves. He could establish us and boast about us before all creation, and He could establish all things and boast about them before the angelic world. The original heart that wanted to boast must begin with me, and through family, society, nation, and the world, my boasting must connect with God's boasting. However, fallen descendants in a position where this cannot happen must understand that they are in a sad position where they must walk the path of establishing the conditions for boasting. 

And Adam and Eve, the conditions for God's boasting, are true sons and daughters that even Satan could boast about. They should have been the original Adam and Eve who are worthy of receiving His love and worship. However, they became offerings for Satan for 6,000 long years. We must understand that God's sorrow as He looked at such humans was immeasurable. 

Now we must establish conditions that can boast before this sorrowful God. One becomes two, two becomes ten, and ten becomes ten thousand, forming nations or states or the world, and we must seek the direction of boasting that God desires. We are fallen descendants who must seek that direction, and we are humans living on this earth today. 

Therefore, you must now realize that it is time to seek the original world where God can boast, the sovereignty where God can boast, the original person whom God can boast about, and the original life, original character, and original love that God can boast about. 

Even Paul, despite having a position and education, did not boast about himself. He had the background to boast about his race, to boast about his denomination, and to boast about his chosen nation, Israel, yet what he truly wanted to boast about in his heart was the conditions of boasting that God wanted to present. You must understand the life of Paul, who fought to hold onto those conditions of boasting that God wanted. 

Moreover, countless ancestors who have been established before God from the time of Noah until now have endured infinite suffering. 

So under what conditions does God deal with us? He establishes the conditions that Satan hates the most to deal with us. This is something we must understand. God emphasized that we should believe in an environment where we could not believe because we had fallen, and He emphasized that we should not eat from a dangerous position where eating could lead to death. 

Thus, our ancestors executed God's word even in environments where it was difficult to believe and practice. Noah believed every day for 120 years even amidst adversity. He firmly expelled all the persecution and ridicule that came upon him. His heart was earnest in wanting to connect with God's heart. He knew that the conditions God wanted to boast about were greater and more precious than any conditions he wanted to boast about himself or any conditions of society. 

Noah was a person whom heaven could boast about. The judgment of Noah established the value of divine boasting and the value of substantial reality. Noah's children were to go through the heart of boasting that God wanted to establish through Noah, but they left that center and thought of themselves as the center. Thus, the heavenly order was turned upside down from there. 

Abraham was the same. Leaving everything behind in Ur of the Chaldeans was not an easy task. Abraham was a person who could live more happily and enjoyably than anyone else in the world of Satan. His wife was extremely beautiful, and his life was abundant. 

God called Abraham, who had the conditions for a rich life and was living more enjoyably than anyone else in the world of Satan, and pushed him into the opposite situation of adversity. You must understand that He commanded him to leave Ur of the Chaldeans, a place where neither his family nor his nation could walk. 

Abraham was a person who deeply felt that there was a heaven that could lead his race and descendants into the world of idealism beyond himself. He knew that the reality of his life was not the standard of boasting for a nation. With this heart, when God's command came to him, he abandoned everything he had. Doing this was not easy. Abandoning his enjoyable family and all his wealth to head toward the wilderness of Haran was a miserable situation for Abraham. However, even if today he appears as a pitiful wanderer, even if today he is in a position and environment where he cannot boast, he walked with the belief that there would one day be a day of boasting.
No matter what adversities and difficulties may come, you must understand that the determination to overcome them a hundred or a thousand times and the heart to seek the garden of glory that heaven desires was greater than anyone else in that era. 

Because there was a point of convergence within the invisible realm of ideals, where God's heart, which was searching for a relative being to boast about, and Abraham's heart aligned, we must recognize that God blessed Abraham with the promise of the absolute ideal garden that He envisioned. 

Thus, Abraham stood before heaven as a blessed ancestor of faith, and his descendants believed that the place they were in at that time was a place to boast about. They were supposed to go beyond their nation and reach out to the world, but they did not realize this. They merely stayed in one place, clinging to their own points of pride, and as a result, they drifted further away from the time when God could boast about the ideals. Consequently, humanity had to go through a sorrowful historical course, which you must understand.

Moses was no different. He lived luxuriously in Pharaoh's palace for 40 years, enjoying life as well as anyone else. However, despite living in an enviable environment, he yearned more than anyone for the day when heaven would establish a nation to boast about. He saw the poor nation of Israel, which had been groaning in misery for 400 years in Egypt, and believed that one day God would surely bless them and lead them to the promised land of Canaan. Moses hoped to build a new garden of hope, a nation that would be as great as any other, a heavenly kingdom that God would boast about.

The reason Moses became the leader of the Israelite nation was that he had no discomfort in a free environment, yet he rejected all of it and did not take it as a condition for pride. Instead, he wanted to boast about the groaning and suffering Israelite nation before heaven. Furthermore, he longed to boast about the land of Canaan, which had been blessed to Abraham, the land that had been taken by the seven nations of Canaan. Because this heart resonated with God's desire to establish the chosen people in the land of Canaan to boast about, God raised Moses before the nation to lead the Israelites.

We must understand that there was such a situation with God. When Moses appeared before the 600,000 people, no one among the Israelites knew that he had such an inner heart. The majority opposed Moses. However, God made it clear through numerous signs and wonders that Moses was the one responsible for leading the Israelite nation to the garden of glory where they could live, allowing them to understand Moses' heart and bringing them out.

Therefore, the Israelite nation should have recognized Moses as the one appointed by heaven and should have been able to boast about him until the end. They should have become such a nation. However, when he appeared in the Pharaoh's palace with divine authority and struck the palace, they rejoiced, saying he was the one appointed by God and our leader, but when they found themselves in the desolate environment of the wilderness, they doubted that he could lead them.

Regarding Moses, whom heaven had set forth as a figure to boast about, the Israelite nation should have known him as their proud leader and representative, understanding that his sorrow was the sorrow of the nation, that the path he walked was the path to resolve the nation's fate, and that leading the nation was also to save the nation. If there had been people who lived centered around Moses, they would not have all collapsed in the wilderness journey.

From the day they resented the Moses they should have boasted about, from the day they betrayed the Moses they should have followed, and from the day they could not honor the Moses they should have served, the pride of heaven, the pride of Moses, and the pride of the nation disappeared. They were supposed to fulfill the purpose through Moses, but they failed to do so. The nation betrayed Moses, who was appointed on their behalf. Here, we must understand that Moses felt a sorrow greater than when he longed for the land of Canaan in Pharaoh's palace.

Moses led the nation out into the wilderness to guide them to the land of hope, Canaan. Even in the environment where the nation rejected and doubted him in the wilderness, Moses' heart of anguish while leading the nation was beyond expression. It was something the entire nation should have been proud of, yet the nation, not knowing or disregarding it, deserved to perish immediately. If the Israelite nation had understood Moses' heart, they would not have been able to complain.

When looking at the starving nation, Moses, in a more serious and poignant position than any starving Israelite, pleaded with heaven for their blessing. Such a heart moved heaven. The Israelite nation never even dreamed that Moses was praying for them, forgetting his own situation.

For the 600,000 Israelites not to perish, they needed to understand that Moses was hungrier and in a more miserable state than they were. They also needed to recognize that Moses was trying to save the nation. Therefore, they were a nation that should have presented Moses as a condition of pride before their descendants for generations to come. Yet, when they instead took a step back and stood in opposition, Moses' heart was indescribably sorrowful.

Furthermore, when the nation did not understand that they should follow Moses' will, who devoted his life to heaven, it was not only Moses who grieved, but heaven grieved even more than Moses. You must understand that heaven's sorrow was greater than Moses' sorrow.

Moses was a leader representing the nation, and although he was someone whom God could boast about more than anyone else, he faced a tragic fate due to the nation's disbelief, and we must recognize this sad circumstance. 

Heaven hoped that the Israelite nation would follow Moses. God wanted them to follow him as much as He raised Moses, but that hope vanished, and the Israelite nation became an unwilling offering to Satan. 

God's hope, which He consistently held for 40 years in Pharaoh's palace, 40 years in the Midian wilderness, and 40 years in the wilderness journey through Moses, disappeared. Thus, the nation and land that could be boasted about vanished. Still, Moses wanted to boast about the incompetent Israelite nation before foreign nations. However, the Israelite nation did not know how to boast about the great Moses whom God had raised.

So what kind of nation will possess the heavenly authority to move the world in the end? What kind of people will they be? You must understand that they will be a people and a nation that can boast about the person whom heaven has raised. Wouldn't that be the case?

Let us think about Jesus. Jesus was the culmination of God's 4,000 years of effort, the embodiment of love and heart. His words, circumstances, hopes, and heart represented the entirety of God's attributes. We must recognize that Jesus was raised as a being who could represent and boast about God's hope.

After enduring a long 4,000 years, God sent Jesus as His representative, a central being to be boasted about, yet even Jesus never boasted about himself while on this earth. 

In a position where God could be pleased, Jesus never had the chance to boast, and no one, to the extent that God could be pleased, ever boasted about Jesus. 

Because Jesus came as a representative of God, he had a deep desire to boast about himself before families, denominations, nations, and the world. Wouldn't that be the case? He came as the fruit of pride that had been awaited for 4,000 years, and thus he had a strong desire to boast about himself before families, societies, nations, and the world.

However, Jesus had no platform to establish himself and boast before the thousands of crowds. God raised him to boast before all creation and even before Satan. Yet, not a single person boasted about him, nor did any family, denomination, or nation boast about him.

Thus, we, the descendants of a tribe that betrayed heaven, are a group that cannot establish dignity and face before heaven. Humanity, which has committed historical sins, cannot stand in a position to boast about themselves and has lost such an environment. Therefore, the fact that we have not yet encountered a person, a denomination, or a nation that can be boasted about is the infinite sorrow of heaven.

When heaven established Jesus to represent 4,000 years of history, He could only weep and say, "How honored I am!" However, what pierced Jesus' heart was that His purpose had not been fulfilled. He lamented, "How could my father's wish, who raised me, end up like this!" and bowed his head before heaven. Therefore, you must understand that the time has come to boast about Jesus, who had such feelings.

The results of the fall due to Adam and Eve's ignorance and God's desire  
We know that the land we live in has flowed down under the power of Satan,  
without being able to see the new morning of God's creation ideology. Our history has been like that,  
and our hearts are the same, and everything we desire and seek is the same.  
In other words, we are deeply asleep under Satan's authority, not knowing how to awaken.  
We are well aware of this fact.  
When God created Adam and Eve and raised His hand to bless them, they were awake,  
and they were in a state where they could enjoy being with God in the eternal ideological world.  
God created Adam and Eve for that purpose. However, Adam and Eve did not clearly grasp  
what kind of relationship they had with God and how to treat all things under the ideology.  
In this incomplete stage, looking forward to completion, they committed the sad error of the fall.  
We know this.  
God told Adam and Eve,  
"If you eat of the fruit of the tree of the knowledge of good and evil, you shall surely die." (Genesis 2:17)  
He also said, "You shall become the masters of all things and the lords of the universe."  
If at that moment the heart of God speaking and the heart of Adam and Eve listening had been completely one,  
the fall would never have happened.  
There was an emotional distance between God, who was speaking, and Adam and Eve, who were listening to the word.  
And Adam and Eve were in a position where they had to fulfill the purpose of the word through a process of growth  
to be able to communicate with God's heart. If Adam and Eve, in that position, had been able to reflect and think again  
about what God's words were and what God's heart was every time they saw all things and angels,  
they would not have fallen. If they had known their position and thought of heaven with an awakened heart,  
they would have been able to discern God's words and the words of the archangel coming from the side.

failed to stand in that position, the temptation of the angel appeared.

heaven knew the entire value of those responsibilities, missions, and what I had to keep and looked at me.

And in the deep sleep, struggling in the world of death, having lost the value of life,

You will feel God's heart, who has recognized humanity countless times.  
At that moment, when you truly realize that heaven exists,  
you will not be able to help but weep with a heart filled with gratitude amidst sorrow.  
How many times has heaven held onto our lives and looked back at us until today!  
Heaven has held onto our life journey and ideological conditions,  
and has looked at us through all the conditions we desire,  
even when we did not know it. Do you know this sorrow of God?  
Have you ever felt the sorrow of heaven, which is incomparable to our own misery and sorrow?  
If you have not, standing at the end of six thousand years of history,  
you will not be able to resolve all of this. It cannot be done.  
Before the hour comes when we can return to the original position of Adam,  
where we can feel God's heart, the fundamental problems of humanity cannot be resolved.  
That is how it is.  
Then we must awaken again and look at the God we believe in.  
We must learn to look at Jesus again.  
We must learn to look again at the countless ancestors who came and went,  
entrusted with the mission of the Holy Spirit and God's providence of restoration.  
We must look again at history, while also looking at this era,  
and think about what will happen in the future.  
If you look up to heaven again and do not have the desire to cry out,  
"O Heaven!" your hopes will be cut off.  
Why are the paths that humanity takes all blocked today?  
Even the clergy, who established religions to guide, cannot solve the fundamental problems and are blocked,  
and the reasons for the blockage of philosophy and science are all because they have not awakened again.  
Since we cannot solve it with what we have held until now, we must abandon that and learn to look at heaven again.  
A heart directed toward heaven and a longing to look at heaven,  
a heart that mourns with that longing,  
and the hearts of those who are dying with that longing will become the cornerstone that can conclude human history.
There may be those who step forward out of concern for the fate of a nation heading towards ruin, but one must not shout for the nation first. One must first cry out to heaven with a heart that is overflowing. Only after that should one cry out for the nation. At such a time, that nation will be saved. History bears witness to this.

Whatever it may be, even if we cannot find it, and even if we struggle without a solution in an unknown world, the day will come when we expel that unknown world and return to our original hearts, awakening from a state of emptiness. That day, that moment will be the moment of creating a new history, the moment when a new life begins, and the moment of rediscovery of a new self. (The recording is briefly interrupted due to a power outage.)

We must recognize that Jesus, who prayed to heaven, was searching for heaven. Therefore, during the 30 years of preparation, Jesus could not show a happy expression even when his brothers were joyful, nor could he rejoice with relatives and neighbors who were happy. You must understand this. Observing the vast difference between the direction desired by heaven and that of all humanity, the greater this difference, the more resolute Jesus became.

You must understand the sorrow of Jesus during those 30 years of preparation when he had many things to say but kept silent. After this 30-year preparation period, Jesus stepped out as a pioneer, saying, "Even if death approaches, I will go; even if the road is tiring, I will go. Even if there are failures, I will go," and he was able to clear his environment. (The recording is briefly interrupted due to a power outage.)

Jesus's attitude towards life

Just as Adam fell by accepting the words that came from the side, we too may perish if we accept the flowing currents of thought in their entirety. Therefore, we must reassess and accept this. If you stand in the position of a master who can feel this through your own heart, life, and static ideals, what ideology could bind you? No ideology could bind you. If this fundamental issue were resolved, peace would have found its way into your heart, and happiness would have entered your living environment. You could have enjoyed freedom and equality.

Even though there are many doctrines today that cry out for ideals, we know well that there has been no doctrine that has granted us mental liberation, emotional liberation, or ideological liberation.

If we lift our eyes again and hope for a day of liberation that awakens our sleeping selves, and if we shake off today's environment and look up to heaven, humanity has not realized until now that there is a master there.

Then, what kind of people are those who have sought God's will throughout history? They were those who cried out, "Oh! Heaven!" and had hearts that soared towards heaven while stepping away from the earth. They were not accepted in their time and stood in the position of outcasts, walking the path of a pitiful life. They were the most pitiful people in the human world. While others lived relying on one another, they had nothing to rely on, no friends to confide in, and no comrades to fight alongside them. They all disappeared.

And after 4,000 years of decline, a young man appeared, who, in order to save all people, first denied the era, denied the environment, and denied the denominations up to that point. What did the young Jesus claim? He proclaimed the will of God that humanity did not know.

Jesus, who bore the will of God, understood that all realities could not become the materials of the overall ideology of life. Therefore, even when the world betrayed him, he kicked away the old and looked at the new self with new eyes, envisioning a new family, society, nation, and world, and he was able to view the new doctrine with dignity. He knew that this value was higher, nobler, and greater than any worldly value, which is why he was not shaken even when Israel betrayed him and the Jewish community turned against him. No matter how much society, family, or any famous scholar betrayed him, or how many storms and trials struck him from all sides, Jesus remained steadfast. He only lifted his eyes again and cried out, "Oh, Heaven!" This was the creed of Jesus's life.

Seeing the environment that denied him, Jesus felt infinite sorrow and realized that God, who looked upon him, was also grieving, feeling a deep sense of remorse. Jesus had a wall of sorrow in his heart for the multitude who rejected the countless prophets sent by God over 4,000 years to establish himself, and he bore a wall of sorrow for the humans who had betrayed God countless times.

Thus, Jesus felt that his own self becoming a sacrificial offering to death was nothing compared to the sorrow God had felt until then and the heart that had fought for humanity. Therefore, he was able to deny himself and bow his head in front of God's heart.

From here, a new awakening of humanity was urged, and the second self began to emerge. Through Jesus, humanity could welcome the spring of revival. Thus, if humanity, which had been in sorrow and dark sleep for 4,000 years, believed in Jesus, it could have welcomed a new spring and revived.

We must have the insight and emotional standards to recognize the Messiah. After Jesus came and went, was there anyone among those who stepped forward for heaven who did not have an attachment to their own life, or who could not feel the sorrow that came to their hearts? However, they felt the sorrow of the master and the fact that the master's life was being torn apart more than their own attachment and sorrow for their lives. Our ancestors were those who had the heart to soar towards heaven, denying everything they had.

Where has the providential path stained with the blood, sweat, and tears of such ancestors gone? It has accompanied the history of humanity until now, but where will it go at the end of history? Will it end here, or will it seek a new direction and go again? In this light, as we face the end times of this providence, if a representative offering of blood, tears, and sweat appears, saying, "Oh, Heaven! Please accept me," he will be the savior of tears, the savior of blood and sweat, and the savior of life in this end time.

If such a person exists to take responsibility for this providence, he will appear on earth with heavenly conditions and will manifest on earth in place of heavenly feelings. When you encounter such a prophet, even if you do not know his heavenly heart and heavenly character, you should at least have a heart that can deny reality and look again.

You must awaken and look again from the position where you live, discerning the second value and the second standard of character that you do not know. If you cannot do this, even if Jesus comes to this earth, you will not recognize him.

Look. Moses, standing before the 600,000 people of Israel, grew up in the palace and was a shepherd in the Midian wilderness. Viewed as he is, he has no value and is no different from the people of the world. However, when Moses appeared with a heavenly heart and a heavenly character, the people of Israel had to open their eyes and look at him again. But because they could not do so, they followed Moses but fell in the wilderness.

The same was true in the time of Jesus, and it is the same today in the end times of history.

The history of sin must be resolved starting from yourselves. If you stand in a position that is a minus to history, it is hell; if you stand in a position that can be a plus to history, it is heaven. Furthermore, when comparing the times with yourselves, if the times are greater than you, it is hell; if you are greater than the times, it is heaven. That is how it is.

Until today, humanity that has followed the fortunes of heaven and earth must restore the day when they can adjust the fortunes of heaven and earth. God has been working through the long span of 6,000 years, looking forward to that one day. The search for a hero who can kick away the sorrows of history that have followed the fortunes of heaven and earth is the providential path of God's 6,000-year restoration.

Therefore, we, who are in a fate that must recover and find this, must have a second set of eyes, feel the second sensation of our lives, seek the second ideal, and equip ourselves with the second character to boast of that value. Only when a being appears who can stand in place of the fortunes of heaven and earth and bless you can the 6,000-year providence come to an end. Furthermore, through that, the conditions under which God can be glorified will be established.

When we recall the image of Jesus praying in the Garden of Gethsemane with three disciples, he was in a solemn posture, trying to move God's heart through the heart of heaven and his own heart. The place where he prayed was the Garden of Gethsemane. Jesus, who had to move the hearts of humanity and integrate heaven and earth, found himself rejected in recognition and was in a position of being expelled from the earth, thus having to forge a connection with heaven. That place was the Garden of Gethsemane.

There were three disciples representing humanity with him in that place, but the feelings Jesus felt were different from those of Peter and the other disciples. Jesus, looking at death while gazing at heaven again, could see beyond the peak of death to the glory of resurrection, but the disciples, who were centered on themselves, did not understand the heart of Jesus, who was immersed in heaven.

This was not a one-time occurrence. They were truly shameless people. This was the behavior of the ancestors who betrayed heaven.

What will remain in the end?

Our True Parents, our master, our bridegroom, the subject of our ideals, the subject of our lives, and the embodiment of heaven who represents us all, were the ancestors who betrayed. Do you feel a deep resentment in your heart towards historical figures as descendants of such ancestors?

When the disciples could not lift their eyes to look at heaven, Jesus must have looked at them several times while praying. The urgency and sorrow in Jesus's heart as he urged them not to fall into temptation were immeasurable. With such feelings, Jesus called upon God and felt God's heart, forgetting himself and thinking of his beloved disciples repeatedly. However, the three disciples were dozing off, unaware of Jesus's heart. This is not merely a representation of the three disciples but a revelation of the inner workings of all humanity.

Today, you are unaware of the solemn and tearful cries of anguish from the Garden of Gethsemane. Even when he cries out to lift your eyes and look again, you cannot hear him. Even when he shakes and strikes to awaken the sleeping humanity, you do not know. There is no one on this earth who understands the sorrowful heart of God, who labors while hoping for a day of blessing when he can find and raise you as his sons and daughters.

Therefore, as original sons and daughters who can live with the ideals of goodness, you must be able to say, "You are my pride, my love, and my standard of happiness," filling the wounds in God's heart and resolving the historical sorrows.

When I look back at myself, who has suffered much sorrow until now, I was in such a wretched state that I could not even be called human. Now, that sorrowful appearance must transform into a joyful, ecstatic, and glorious form that can dance as the second self. If such a thing does not appear on this earth, you must understand that God is a pitiful God.

Now we are in a fate that requires us to deny ourselves and receive a new recognition. However, the land we live on and our lives here do not yield any heavenly income for us.

So, even if the world goes, friends go, parents go, spouses go, and everything on the earth goes, you must be able to say that this earnest heart that looks up to heaven cannot go.

You must be able to say that just as God is an unchanging being, I too cannot change. You must hold onto the heavenly connection and the connection of blessings, even if it means leaving behind your circumstances on this earth.


Even if my heart is torn and I become a sacrifice of Satan, I long to possess God's love. I hope that the heart that can drive away the conditions of the fall remains within me. Have I become the one that heaven has been searching for? Have I become someone who can show myself before heaven? Have I become someone who can boast before heaven and earth?

Heaven! Come down. Humanity! Gather together. All creation! I must become someone who can dance and sing. 

Thus, I must become the condition through which the grievances of heaven are resolved, the grievances of the earth are resolved, the grievances of all creation are resolved, and all sorrow that has pierced the heart of the Creator is healed. I must be able to sing on behalf of heaven, sing on behalf of the earth, and sing on behalf of the entire universe. I must be able to earnestly ask that only the heart of loyal devotion remains with us, so that we can command Satan. Only those who possess that heart can become the masters of history; only those who possess that heart can move the history of humanity. That heart must become the target of hope for our descendants, and you must realize that you have the mission to pass on such a heart.

For this reason, Jesus fought for this ideal, our ancestors fought for this ideal, and God is looking down upon the earth and awakening humanity from the realm of darkness for this ideal. 

Who will break through the historical barriers of misfortune and awaken the hearts of sleeping humanity through the heart of heaven? Who will awaken their own sleeping selves? Who will introduce the explosive heart of heaven's love? It is you, who may seem insignificant. Therefore, even if you are pushed and chased and wander in despair, you must consider that you are the vanguard who must connect with that one point.

Having been called to stand before heaven, earth, and all creation with such responsibility, we must fulfill that mission and responsibility, resolving the grievances of heaven and earth, and as the second hope of heaven and earth, we must become a form that allows God to forget all grievances and look upon us again with a joyful heart. I must become someone whom humanity can look upon with joy, and I must become a being that all creation can rejoice in and look upon.

That is the garden of ideals, that is the original heaven, and the place where we unite centered on one ideal is the earthly heaven. Heaven has awakened us countless times to introduce this.

However, we have forgotten this, so you must become those who engrave this sorrow in your hearts and strive to find the second self to take responsibility for it.
