We know that there was a responsibility for Jesus to establish the conditions of relationships on this earth.

Today, with such a heart at the center, let us abandon everything of the earth, and even if we must fall with only the standard of the heavenly realm, may the hope that Jesus desired, the hope that heaven desires, and the hope that humanity desires be fulfilled on earth because of us. May we be sons and daughters who can run towards that day, dedicating our lives without reservation, whether it is today, tomorrow, one year, or ten years. We earnestly ask and pray in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

Hope for the Ideal Heaven
Matthew 3:1-17
<Prayer (I)> We know how much our Father has labored throughout the long years to restore the original true person. We ask that at this time, we may feel in our hearts and bodies that He has come over the bloody peaks of history, longing for the original Adam and Eve.

We also know that our ancestors, who have inherited this work and upheld the will of providence, have walked the sorrowful path of the cross in every place they went. 

We are aware that we have a historical and providential responsibility that we must carry on this path of the cross, which remains for us today. We ask that you inspire us again with your strength and your counsel. May we overcome the remaining peaks of this cross and become those who can sing of the Father's glory in the original garden that He desired.

We know that everything belonging to us is not eternal, so grant us the heavenly determination to break through the peaks of the cross that are blocking us from fulfilling what remains today. We earnestly hope and desire this, beloved Father.

To fulfill this work, it has come to the time when we must step forward with a solemn determination, as if we are going into battle with swords drawn. Beloved Father! Please allow us to devote all our energy to fighting today, tomorrow, and at any time, and grant us the strength to fight against the many Satans that block our path. We earnestly hope and desire this.

May we appear victorious on the battlefield and be allowed to live with the Father in the garden of His glory. May we become your sons and daughters who can fulfill the overall will that the Father desires and sing of the Father's love, and may we be allowed to be the sons and daughters that the Father seeks, who can be presented and boasted of before the world of Satan and all creation.

Thus, as sons and daughters found before the Father, may we be able to dwell with the Father forever, and as those who have fulfilled the Father's work, the Father's ideology, and the Father's desires, may we be true children who can comfort the Father with songs of joy and glory. We earnestly hope and desire this, beloved Father.

May we become those who can sing of the Father's glory through the remaining path of struggle and the remaining path of the cross. Beloved Father! We earnestly hope and desire this.

This day is a holy day. May all people come together to uphold the overall will of the Father, and may the time come quickly when all people can move to build the Father's victorious nation.

Please bless our thirty million people, and bestow a special hand of grace upon your sons and daughters gathered here today.

Embrace this nation with a heart of love, and may we become a nation that moves according to your urging, fulfilling the overall will of the Father and the remaining grievances through our struggles and victories, manifesting the glory of that fulfillment until the time comes.

We have gathered before the Father today with our insufficient and imperfect selves, so please remove all that is unworthy and allow only that which belongs to our original nature to manifest at this time. May this gathering be one that can be offered before the Father as the form that heaven desires, connecting only with the original glory in each heart, and may it be allowed to be taken only as the Father's.

Please be with the countless sons and daughters scattered throughout the world, and we ask that you work with them as well. We pray in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

<Prayer (II)> Beloved Father, you have called us together, so please do not leave us behind at this time. We thank you for allowing us to come this far amidst many trials. We know well that you guide us on this path for our sake. We also know that there is a historical responsibility that must be fulfilled through us, as the sorrow of heaven and the sorrow of the earth must be resolved through us.

We are grateful for the grace that allows us to call you Father in this place today, through the words you have permitted, the grace you have granted, and the life you have given.

We know how precious the responsibility entrusted to us today is, so beloved Father! Please do not abandon us at this time, but once again embrace us in your bosom and transfer the heart you desired to share with us into our hearts. Please entrust to us the overall will you wished to pass on, so that we may become those in whom you can find peace.

Now, please do not allow our hearts and bodies to belong only to ourselves, but let this time be one in which we can move as your own. May it be a time that becomes an altar where you can preside, where nothing other than what belongs to you is permitted.

Countless Satans are eager to block our movements. At this time, we are eagerly anticipating the heavenly power and ability to overcome this with all our hearts and bodies, so beloved Father! Please grant us strength and bestow grace upon us, so that we may become heavenly soldiers who can stand before the power of death with the authority of resurrection. We earnestly hope and desire this, beloved Father.

Beloved Father! Through the training period you have granted us, we have received training and scattered your sons and daughters throughout the three thousand ri. Please open the way for them, grant them strength when they fight, and allow them to establish the authority of heaven through faith. Please allow them to be sufficient in exercising the actual power of heaven. We earnestly hope and desire this, beloved Father.

Grant them the ability to drive away enemies with the words of the iron cage and the shield of life, and bestow upon them the glory of heavenly victory. We earnestly hope and desire this, beloved Father.

We already know that the time has come to resolve the heart of the Father, who has endured for six thousand years, and you have already signaled that time to us, so please do not let this work return in vain. May there be movements of life upon all that moves, and may the sovereign work of heaven be manifested wherever it appears. Please allow them to take on the form of life, and allow us to meet the day when enemies can be silenced and subdued. We earnestly hope and desire this, beloved Father.

This day is the promised day, so please bless it, and since it is the day you have permitted, may your will be manifested. Please transfer the hidden heart of the Father's love into our hearts, so that we may be able to sing of the Father's grace. Allow us to reveal the Father's glory. May this time be one in which we can offer true worship before the Father. We earnestly hope and desire this, beloved Father.

Please allow us to awaken the thirty million people who are asleep, and grant us the ability to awaken the countless people of humanity on this earth. We know that you are concerned for them wherever they are, and we also know that you are holding them up to prevent them from falling. So, please allow us to hold onto this nation and to fight for this humanity.

We understand that they are not here for us, but that we are here for them, and we know that you are still fighting for them. If we are to live not for ourselves but for you, please guide us to feel the urgent sense of responsibility for your will and for all humanity. 

We earnestly hope and desire that we may become heavenly soldiers who can fight for the will of the Father, cherishing every moment to fulfill this mission and responsibility. 

Please bless the many altars that gather today on behalf of all people, and we know that there are many hidden sons and daughters who are building lonely altars and appealing before the Father, so please grant them special grace.

At the end of the day, please signal the will of heaven, and may the time of the Father's glory come.
Please allow us to give them a warning. Please grant that the day when we can gather around the gifts of heaven may come quickly, so that all nations can prepare one altar to sing praises to the Father and worship before Him. We earnestly hope and wish for the day to come upon the whole earth.

Please allow a glorious day of providence to arrive quickly, and grant that the day of joyful victory may come soon for us who are fighting in hope of that day. We earnestly hope and wish, Father, that the glory of heaven and the joy of victory may soon be realized on earth.

Please personally oversee all the time from this moment onward. We have gathered here at this time, so please remove all our assertions and the concepts we feel, allowing us to be united in a heavenly heart. We earnestly ask that we may be completely captivated by You, and we pray all these words in Your name. Amen.

<Prayer (Ⅲ)> Father! Please allow us, who have gathered here today, to become the sorrowful crowd that gathered by the Jordan River. Please allow us to become the crowd that gathered before John the Baptist to hear the new news from heaven.

We, who are examining the footsteps of the Israelite people who awaited the Messiah with earnest hearts, hope and wish to become like the crowd that was intertwined and moved around John the Baptist, the crowd that followed Jesus, and the crowd that rejoiced in a new hope by connecting hearts.

We know that the sad tears of the Father, lamenting where the chosen people of Israel, who boasted of their authority as the chosen people and lived within the blessing, have gone, remain on this earth.

We understand that even though the Father has endured historical sorrow for 4,000 years, holding on to the chosen people of Israel to send the Messiah, they have embraced the Messiah in the arms of Satan. We come to know that the Father’s sorrow is not just the sorrow of that time, but remains as the sorrow of countless millennia of history.

When we recall that the chosen people of Israel at that time did not know this fact, we cannot help but feel sorrow that we have the responsibility to expose the historical crimes and repent for the historical sins.

Father, please stretch out Your hand. Father, please reveal the heart of love. Father, please move Your weary steps and come to us. We earnestly hope and wish for this.

Jesus came to find the nation that was collapsing with the sorrowful heart of heaven, and He had compassion on them, not sparing His own life. However, the Israelite people, who claimed to be the chosen nation, treated the Messiah sent by heaven and the prepared John the Baptist as they pleased, hiding them in the shadow of historical sorrow. Today, we know this fact.

Please allow us, Your sons and daughters gathered here today, to understand that the Israelite people at that time did not betray heaven because they were inferior to us, nor did they forget heaven because their hearts were less devoted than ours. They lacked hope for a new era, and though they expected the Lord to come with the ideology of a new Messiah, they rejected the Messiah who appeared in a very humble, pitiful, and insignificant form.

Now, please allow us to examine what position we are in. Today, we often criticize the historical Israelite people and enjoy criticizing the circumstances of that time, but please let us realize that the circumstances then and now are not different.

If we had been there at that time, we would have been among them, and if we had lived in that era, we would have been in the same position as them. Please grant us a heart that acknowledges that we bear the traces of such historical sins and that the claws of Satan are targeting our bodies at this time, Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this.

There are many times when we lose the authority of life and struggle without even realizing it, so please break through all these contradictory environments today and suppress all circumstances bound by the environment, so that we do not create a stepping stone for Satan to rejoice, but become a heart offering that can relieve the Father’s sorrow.

Whom do we come to see in this place? Whom do we seek in this place? What we truly desire and seek is the heart of the Father. Please allow us to be a gathering that seeks the heart of the Father revealed through the prophet rather than a crowd that seeks some historical teacher.

O Father! In our hearts remain the bitter roots of sin that have been defiled by the world, and our bodies have been wounded by the invasion of Satan. Please appear with a heart of compassion and embrace us, the pitiful ones, in Your bosom for this one hour. Please allow this time to be when we are intoxicated by Your eternal life, transcending all our perceptions, and can face You with the original character.

Please help us find the ideals of the heavenly kingdom that You have left behind, and allow the joyful news of the new nation that You have left behind to find us. Please let the sound of liberation ring out and the day come quickly when we can rejoice and dance before the gifts of freedom and liberation. We earnestly hope and wish that a new garden of joy may unfold before humanity.

Now, please oversee the remaining time and reveal the words that You wish to manifest according to Your will. Please remove the shadow of dark Satan and let this hour be one in which we can establish a heavenly connection that can introduce the joy of having received true life, and let this time be one in which the dead bodies receive the grace of resurrection and can recognize the Father. We earnestly hope and wish for the words of recreation and the movements of the life of recreation to be manifested here, and we pray all these words in Your name. Amen.

<Word> We humans have been longing for the lost ideal nation since the day of the fall, and we are well aware that we have been fighting through infinite hardships while harboring new hopes.

Even though the surroundings we live in should be happy, we also know very well that we are struggling in unhappiness, unable to connect with all the conditions and relationships of happiness that we long for in our hearts.

We must recall that standing in such a position is because humanity has lost the heavenly kingdom that God created as the ideal.

God created all things in six days. Among them, Adam and Eve were created as the protagonists of all creation. Adam and Eve were able to govern all created things on behalf of God in the garden of creation, enjoying the glory of God, and were the center of glory, victory, and joy before heaven and earth. They appeared before heaven and earth in this form, but they lost their position and failed to fulfill their responsibilities. Thus, we know that from that day, this earth became a land of sorrow, pain, and death.

If someone were to appear and deny this fact, claiming that it is not so under any conditions, we could say that he is one who denies his own heart, denies historical facts, and denies the realistic life we live.

Therefore, it is time for all humans today to remember that they live in an uneasy and chaotic land, in an environment filled with fear and death.

We must become aware of this and awaken to a new realization, removing the contradictions of reality and being filled with a new heart, and we must have a new ideology and hope. If we acknowledge that there is a Creator, we must have the determination to fight alongside that ideology throughout our lives, today and tomorrow, to break through this contradictory environment and establish a heavenly connection.

Though it is a path of death that cannot be avoided, and an environment of pain that cannot be escaped, we must have a heart that can deny all of this and a hope that can step forward to deny everything. We must forget all this and run toward the new ideal garden, which is the purpose we must pursue and establish at the end of history or in the course of history. We must know this.

This is what God hopes for, what humanity hopes for, and what this nation and we today hope for. From this standpoint, you must feel that you have to bear the responsibility for it today. Therefore, the title I wish to speak to you today is "The Ideal Heavenly Kingdom of Hope."

As a result of human fall, God's hope was broken, and human hope was also severed. The human being, who is the object of God's hope, should have been able to move heaven and earth as a protagonist representing the universe, as an individual of the heavenly ideology, and as an ideal individual, a complete offering. However, because humanity could not become such beings, hope remained for us and hope remained for God.

When we think about this, the creation garden that was created for humanity, the creation ideology to enjoy happiness with humanity, is determined by ourselves. We must recall this fact once again and take responsibility for it and fight to resolve God's historical resentment.

If it is sad, there is no sadness greater than this; if it is unjust, there is no greater injustice; if it is anger, there is no greater anger. We must realize that the time when this psychological shock explodes from within you is the time when you can seek new ideologies and hopes.

Therefore, we must not forget that heaven has been fighting until this time to bring a new shock to the hearts of fallen humans. Many prophets and sages who took on the mission of heaven fought and died to awaken humanity, which was asleep in the realm of death, to the fact that there is a world of new ideology and a garden of new hope, and to give them the shock to deny all the environments they have lived in until now.

We must understand that there has been no group, nation, or humanity that has stepped forward based on the words of warning given by our prophets and sages throughout history. Even though we should mourn this historical crime, today we cannot even recognize this crime.

We know that Jacob had a wilderness life of 21 years that he did not want. He had the standard of heart that could overcome all the difficulties he faced during those 21 years. That is, the firm heart toward heaven and the heart impacted by heaven's shock could govern his life and dominate his existence, allowing him to overcome all the environmental hardships and boldly traverse the path of restoration.

Jacob, who went forth without caring about all the pains and difficulties that befell him with the determination of that day when he received heaven's shock, was indeed a figure of faith who blocked the history of Abraham, the father of faith, who had made mistakes and defeated Satan.

Moses, who was born with the responsibility of the nation, could not be governed by the luxurious life of Pharaoh's palace. Although Moses lived a poor shepherd's life in the Midian wilderness for 40 years, that environment could not conquer the psychological shock that had permeated his heart. Because Moses had a rising psychological shock that desired to connect with heaven beyond the nation, humanity, and the world, he could smoothly pass through the 40 years in the Midian wilderness.

What was it that our ancestors earnestly longed for? It was a new nation, a place where God resides. We know that they fought to establish this.

Even during the favorable 40 years when Moses led 600,000 people into the wilderness, the surrounding environment was very difficult. However, he was able to lead the 600,000 people into Canaan because the heart that longed to enter the promised land of Canaan was stronger than the hearts of the 600,000 people who opposed him.

The Purpose of Heaven and the Efforts of Our Ancestors

Furthermore, Jesus Christ, who came as the central being that heaven hoped for over 4,000 years, to introduce the ideal of the heavenly kingdom to humanity and to fulfill that ideology, did not become immersed in the words of the environment of that time. He was not satisfied with the lifestyle of that social environment, nor was he trapped in the customs of the conscious Jewish community that were bound by forms and regulations.

When Jesus appeared with a new standard of heart and a new word centered around that, denying all historical things, and presented new actions along with that word, we know that historical figures, historical organizations, and all nations rose in rebellion against Jesus.

We must realize through history that this was the obstacle in the path of the Christ seeking the ideology.

We live in a time when everyone is saying it is the end. We are in a position where we cannot boast of our own existence at a time when all humanity is facing life and death. Therefore, if each of us does not receive a new shock of heart with the ideology introduced by Jesus 2,000 years ago, and if those of us living on the old system do not cause a new explosion of heart, this era cannot escape from the pit of historical sorrow.

We are at the end of history, and we have learned all the words we can learn through the Bible. Countless scholars have devoted themselves to studying the Bible for 2,000 years, but it has ended there. All these movements that claimed to be perfect seem to have developed and presented an ideal ideology to humanity, but they were not the heavenly ideology that humanity truly desires, nor were they a new movement that could open the garden of the heart. We can see this from reality. Now we must become those who can break down these barriers and navigate through them.

Then, now humanity, regardless of you or me, is all in despair.
What is the problem? It is that there is a Creator, and if that Creator exists, there must be a heaven that He wishes to establish, and the question is how to introduce that heavenly ideology to humanity. However, since the existing ideologies are insufficient, there is a need for a new ideology, and those who merely seek something new without having the heart to admire that new ideology are to be regarded as historical criminals.

If you hope for a new ideology to emerge and wish for all humanity to be happy, the question is whether you have the determination to overcome all grievances and fight against all realities.

The issue of introducing a new ideology
What I want to ask you is, where is the ideology that can break the historical stubbornness that still has not been overcome, that can create a new shock and ignite a passion for a new ideology? If there is a heaven, can such an ideology be introduced to us without reservation? Have you ever thought about this? If you have not, you must realize that you are a shameful sinner before our ancestors who struggled and sought after the ideal world, the garden of this ideology.

With a heart yearning for heaven, feel in your heart the world of the new creative ideology, the world of hope that humanity must seek, and it was Jesus who could act upon that feeling of shock, saying, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is at hand!"

But what was the environment like when Jesus acted upon this shock? The more Jesus moved forward, the more all people should have welcomed Him, yet the environment was such that no one welcomed Him. Not only at that time but even until now, countless people in history and many spirits in the spirit world did not understand the words Jesus cried out and His historical actions, nor did they know what Jesus' responsibilities were. Thus, there was no one to welcome Jesus.

However, Jesus, who brought a new ideology, felt deeply that in order to establish that ideology, He had to overcome all opposing conditions that came upon Him until the purpose of that ideology was fulfilled. The stronger the shock from the ideology, the more resolute His determination was to repel all adverse conditions from the environment, which is why Jesus could overcome any environment He faced.

Today, we are yearning for something in our hearts. Our bodies are struggling to find something. We are also groaning in fear and anxiety. In such times, we must recognize that we should long for the day when we can break free from all these conditions of fear and anxiety.

Today, we are not the only ones in such an environment. Jesus Christ, who came 2,000 years ago, was also in such an environment. Reflecting on this fact, think about how Jesus navigated through that environment.

When Jesus came to this earth, He knew that all things were created by God, and that those created things should have been governed by the true owner to establish the ideal kingdom of heaven. However, due to human fall, the ideal kingdom that the Creator desired turned into hell on earth, a world of indescribable fear and anxiety, a world of conflict. Therefore, Jesus began His public life not to possess that ideology and ideal kingdom but to take responsibility for and save this hellish world.

As Jesus moved toward the ideal kingdom, He faced unimaginable loneliness, adversity, and sorrow. Yet, knowing that this was the path He had to take, He resolved to continue until the ideal garden was established, until He could meet the Creator on behalf of humanity in that garden. You must feel this. We, too, must go toward that ideal garden.

Now, if you have received this shock, along with that shock, you must have the heart that says, "Father! I want to go! I want to go toward the ideal kingdom of hope!"

The path to the ideal kingdom of hope is not a smooth one; it is a sorrowful path. The way to heaven does not start from heaven but begins in the world of sin. We must understand that we must start from hell, the world of sin, and break free from that hell to connect with heaven.

We are destined to go. We are destined to go toward the ideal kingdom of hope. Let us think about Jesus, who had to walk this path. What kind of path did Jesus walk? He did not walk a smooth path. Jesus did not take a path that was welcomed by the masses. Although Jesus was the Savior of all people and the protagonist of the universe, He never once acted as a protagonist nor did He boast of Himself to declare to the masses to follow Him.

Jesus walked the path of suffering
In walking the path of providence, Jesus, who should have led the way, stood at the back of the nation, saying, "You all take the comfortable path. I will take the hardest path," taking on the difficulties of the nation and the world, bearing the cross of suffering that humanity despised. Jesus knew that the path He had to take was a historically sorrowful path, a path entangled with adverse conditions, and yet He walked with a solemn mental resolve during the 30 years of preparation and the 3 years of public life. The more solemn that resolve was, the more He became a friend to the sorrowful humanity, and as He witnessed humanity struggling in fear and being trampled by Satan, He fought against Satan from the lowest historical position, from the lowest position of the era.

If there is sorrow among humanity, He walked with the heart that said, "I will take that upon myself." If there is difficulty among humanity, He walked with the heart that said, "I will take that upon myself." If there is death among humanity, He walked with the heart that said, "I will take that upon myself." His footsteps were personal, yet His mission was historical, epochal, and future-oriented.

Then, where did Jesus, who bore the responsibility to understand the heart of God after creation and the heart of humanity, and the heart of all created beings, walk toward? He did not seek a luxurious palace, nor did He go to the house of any dignitary enjoying glory and power. Knowing that the conditions of the time were not prepared, Jesus sought the opposite path.

He knew that the path the Jewish community, representing Israel, which had believed for 4,000 years, should take to connect with heaven was blocked, and although He tried to open that path of hope, He had no choice but to seek the rear of the nation because they did not believe.

Jesus, who had to go toward the kingdom of hope, had to lead the world beyond individuals, families, nations, and countries toward heaven, the world of ideology. Jesus stood at the forefront of the nation with that ideology but was chased away by the nation. He was expelled from the religious community. He was chased away by His family. He was even chased away by His disciples and mocked by robbers. How sorrowful must have been Jesus' heart at that time!

Jesus, who had to advance with the ideology of the Father, who had to introduce the garden of happiness to all humanity, had to walk the path of opposition. What must have been the appearance and heart of Jesus? If He could not go directly to where He had to go, He had to turn around and go. After 4,000 years of history had passed, He had to turn back and walk that path. This was Jesus' mission and responsibility, which is why He prayed to God many times.

If there are obstacles preventing the fulfillment of the Father's will, He would turn away from them and walk the path that would take thousands of years. He would go only toward the garden of hope. "Father, I am here, so do not be discouraged."

However, the nation established by heaven, the religious community established by heaven, the family established by heaven, and even John the Baptist and his followers all blocked Jesus' path and betrayed Him. In this situation, God, who was watching Jesus, felt ashamed before Him. Wouldn't He?

When all the environmental conditions that had been prepared for 4,000 years to welcome the Messiah collapsed at once, Jesus stood in a position to comfort the sorrowful God. Since God was sad, Jesus must have been sad as well, yet He stood in a position where He had to deny His own sorrow and comfort heaven. Jesus was treated as an enemy by His nation, labeled a heretic by the religious community, accused of betrayal by His family, and mocked even by robbers.

Eventually, He bore the cross and, while being nailed to the cross on Golgotha, opened His mouth for those who sought to kill Him, saying, "Father, forgive them, for they do not know what they do."

Jesus, who vowed to go toward the garden of heaven's ideology, had to walk a path that did not end in glory, happiness, and joy, but rather ended in sorrow, injustice, resentment, and death. He had to go toward the garden of ideology that the Father sought. Jesus' journey toward that garden of ideology was on behalf of humanity, on behalf of history, and on behalf of all created beings. Therefore, we who follow Jesus are also destined to go. If we cannot go while alive, we are destined to go even in death.

Christianity is the community of the cross
Jesus took on the sufferings of humanity and started from the lowest position of humanity, ultimately reaching the summit of Golgotha. That place was where Jesus sacrificed everything about Himself. Oh! Where did the Son of God, the heavenly prince, the appearance of the heavenly royal heir go? Where did the Messiah of humanity, the Savior of humanity go? That place was one where He could not claim even an ounce of His own value. However, Jesus was able to look toward heaven and go toward the garden of heaven's ideology, overcoming the hill of death because His ideology was stronger than the power of death and stronger than any historical force. Thus, the resurrection occurred, breaking the power of death, and He was able to lead opposing humans to repentance, allowing today's Christianity to establish a foundation of victory.

We, who must follow the path taken by Jesus, must go whether we live or die. The question is whether you have the heart that longs to go.

Regardless of what shock you receive, you must have the desire to go toward that ideology. Whether you eat or starve, whether you are beaten or scorned, whether you are persecuted, you must have a feeling greater than the power of death that says, "I want to go." If you do not have that desire, you cannot overcome the power of death in the great judgment that appears at the end of history. You must have the heart that says, "I will go no matter what, whether it is this way or that way. Father, I know You are here, and I know the world is like this, so even if no one else goes, I will go."

However, the path is not smooth. Humanity's ancestors did not start from a place of peace, happiness, and joy; they started from sorrow, grief, adversity, fear, and anxiety. Therefore, we, who are at the final stage of atonement, must also walk all those historical sorrowful paths. Unless a Messiah appears to introduce a heavenly ideology that can lead us out of all the foundations of sin in this era, humanity will have no way to escape from anxiety, fear, and the power of death. There is no way to live.

That is why Christianity is originally a community of sacrifice. It is a community of the cross. It is a community of bloodshed. It is a community of service. It is a community that steps forward to die first. Christianity, which has emerged from heaven, has illuminated its tradition through this historical process, and if today's Christianity lacks this, it must face divine punishment. This is a conclusion we can draw.

Christianity, which must pioneer the destiny of the world, must become a shepherd and a flock that can cry out with the heart of Jesus, who bled on the summit of Golgotha, saying, "Forgive them their sins," and introduce a new ideology, new hope, and a new ideal garden. You must understand that you must become such a person.

Moreover, just as Peter, James, and John, who represented the nation of Israel, did not know that Jesus, who died on the cross at Golgotha, would resurrect, if there are shepherds and flocks willing to appear before heaven, even at the cost of their lives, they must understand that they are beings who can connect the new era and the new heavenly ideology.

Today, we must keep in mind that we must reassess everything around us. We must reassess any emerging leader. The Jewish priests, what kind of group were they? They were a group that trampled on the heavenly new message. We must reassess what governs us today and what spiritually controls our nation.

We must break down the foundations of all the sins of this era and understand that if you do not receive the shock that can ignite a new ideology leading to new hope through your community, that community cannot escape the judgment that the first Israel faced.

Humans must meet God
We must go. We must transcend the faith ideologies of established churches or adherents of other religions. We must go beyond the cross of Jesus and, furthermore, not only the cross but also the heart of Jesus' resurrection, and we must go beyond to the heart of God to become sons and daughters who can comfort Him. We must reach that place.

Where can our footsteps lead us, to that place we want to go, the place where the Father is, the place where the Lord is, the place where the true form of humanity exists? No matter what holds us back on this earth, we must walk the path of ideology, overcoming all conditions that block our way, and we must lead them along that path.

We are those who must bear this responsibility and go. God has already sought us for 6,000 years. We are destined to go, and heaven is destined to come to us.

Heaven has made indescribable efforts to come to us. Have you thought about the efforts of heaven? From the day of the fall, there has never been a time when God did not follow Adam and his descendants, and today, without you knowing, God is tirelessly seeking you. Have you looked for that heaven? You must understand that there are 6,000 years of sorrow and countless hills of death blocking the way. Just as heaven has walked this path to find us, we must have the heart to walk this path to reach heaven.

Jesus did not come to seek any ideology for Himself. Jesus came to introduce the garden of happiness and hope to all humanity. Therefore, He labored for all humanity, and for all humanity...
You have suffered pain and walked the path of sorrow for all mankind. Because of this, there is no being in all creation, in heaven or on earth, that is unrelated to Jesus's sorrow; however, He had no way to go. Yet, Jesus did not mourn and die there; instead, He left behind new hope. Thus, He became the master who completed the standard of the Messiah and pioneered the garden of new hope. We must understand this.

Until today, we did not know this Jesus. But it turns out that Jesus was someone who left with resentment and grievance. Now that we know, we must seek out the Jesus that we have cast aside. And we must meet Him. You should have a deep longing to find this Jesus and a desperate desire to meet Him. Just as Jesus fought holding onto God's hand to meet the God who has worked for 4,000 years, you should have a heartfelt desire to meet the heavenly figure who represents 6,000 years of history after Jesus. You can meet the God and Jesus who comforted you when you were sad, helped you when you were in difficulty, and took your grievances and resentments upon themselves. There are twists and turns in meeting them.

When Jesus was about to die, He made various requests to humanity. He said that He had prepared a place for us in heaven. He also promised us the day we would meet again. We still have steps to take and a day to meet. Therefore, it is not enough to just have the determination to go. We must meet.

The day we meet will be the end of history, and from a Christian perspective, it will be the day of the Second Coming. Therefore, you must have the desire to welcome that day of the Second Coming and the determination to break through to the gates of hell, which are under the power of suffering, persecution, and grievances. The place where all conditions that Satan can accuse are removed and where God’s ideals move is heaven. The place where the conditions of suffering are completely removed and where we can start with joy is heaven. Therefore, if we leave behind the path of suffering we must take on earth, we will suffer in the spirit world for what we have left behind.

We humans are in a position where we can only meet after we have walked the entire path we must take. After we have walked the historical path that Jesus walked first, who will we meet?

**The Responsibility of the Bride (Believers)**

God has prepared for 2,000 years to meet after Jesus came and went. Jesus has been praying for us before God in the spirit world for 2,000 years to meet the bride of heaven at the end. The Jesus who has gone has a field of responsibility as the bridegroom, and the humans on earth have a field of responsibility as the bride. For this reason, we know through the Bible that the bridegroom, Jesus, has been working hard for 2,000 years to fulfill that responsibility.

So how will the brides left on earth meet the bridegroom? First, they must fulfill their responsibilities. Jesus also fulfills His responsibility to appear on earth and then appears. Therefore, we must fulfill our responsibilities. Then, as a reward, we will receive the gifts of heaven. That is why the Christians of the entire world in the position of the bride must fulfill their responsibilities as brides.

Jesus said, "You will be my witnesses to the ends of the earth." (Acts 1:8) He also said, "Whoever wants to save their life will lose it, but whoever loses their life for me will find it." (Matthew 16:25)

We must become a group that fights to fulfill our responsibilities. Only then will we not be ashamed before the hearts of those who have fought for the earth, just like the bridegroom Jesus, who could not eat or find peace of mind for even a day to fulfill His responsibility. We must understand that only after each person has fulfilled their responsibilities can they qualify to meet Jesus.

Until today, there has not been a single person among fallen humanity who has fulfilled the responsibility to meet God, which is why no one has entered heaven. Jesus is also in paradise. Paradise is the waiting room for entering heaven.

So what is the hope of humanity? It is to be able to resolve the grievances of the fall and to be able to say that we have fulfilled our responsibilities as humans after going through the path of restoration. That is the image that Jesus has been preparing for 2,000 years and is seeking.

With a longing to meet such Jesus, we must clear away the historical conditions of Jesus's sorrow in our daily lives. We must be able to walk the path of all the adversities that Jesus walked with victory and joy.

Today, Christians must understand that they should meet Jesus from the position of having fulfilled the responsibility of pioneering the path of victory that clears the way to Golgotha.

Where is the heart that wants to see? Where is the heart that wants to go? We are those who have neither a heart to see nor a heart to go. Even if we are torn apart and killed in the place of our longing to see, there must be a group of people on earth who have a desperate heart that can overcome that with their longing to see. Only then can we face the Jesus who has longed to see us for 2,000 years.

"We long to see! O heaven! What was Jesus's desire? His desire was for this earth and heaven to become the ideal kingdom of heaven. For that kingdom of heaven to be built, there must be a people who can live in heaven, a land that can establish heaven, the sovereignty of heaven, and a ruler who can move that sovereignty. May all people living on this earth become the citizens of heaven. That is what we long for."

Even if this earth is vast, there is not a single piece of land that God can claim as His own. There is no land that Jesus can claim as His own. Jesus did not have a single piece of land that could be said to be free from Satan's invasion.

The ideal of such Jesus is the ideal of heaven and the ideal of the earthly kingdom that must be established on earth. Because there must be a group of people who long for that ideal and want to become God's people, Jesus said to seek. He said to ask. He said to knock on the door.

**We Must Fight to Build the Kingdom of Heaven**

As we break through the path of grievances left on this earth, you must understand that only with a deep longing to see the world of ideals that Jesus yearns for can you meet the reality of that ideal.

After the first Israel fell, Christians around the world have been working hard to bring forth the country, the people, the land, the sovereignty, and the ruler that Jesus longed for as the second Israel. However, since reality does not align with that ideal, if there is sorrow, there is no greater sorrow than this.

What kind of person is a patriot? A patriot is someone who feels the pain of their people more than their own pain, someone who feels more pain than having their own body torn apart when they see their land being violated, and someone who feels more grievance and pity than their own grievances and pity when they see their sovereign or ruler in a pitiful and unjust situation.

Yet, why do we have the humble words that we are brides who are to meet the heavenly prince? We are in a state of unfaithfulness, unworthiness, and sinfulness, unable to even face the Word. Therefore, when we see the heavenly people being violated and this land being trampled by Satan, we must fight to restore this, even if it costs us our lives. We must understand that we have a heavenly mission to restore the sovereignty of goodness.

Christians today must recognize that the time has come to eradicate the wicked on earth with a conscience of ideals. We must understand what the day that Jesus desires and longs for looks like. There must be a heart that longs to see and meet the land, the people, the sovereignty, and the ruler of the ideals that Jesus longed for during His lifetime, and there must be a heart that wants to see that kingdom before my eyes are filled with dust and before my body disappears.

If there is someone who has such a heart, that kingdom will never perish. With such a heart, we must want to create the land of heaven. We must want to restore the sovereignty of goodness. We must be able to say that we want to be faithful before such a Lord.

As the times grow tighter, we must deeply feel the tremendous fact that our fate is placed at the pivotal point of history. This time has come. For whom do you exist? You may think you exist for yourself, but you do not exist for yourself. You may think you exist for your family, but you do not exist for your family. You may think you exist for your nation and the world, but you do not exist for your nation and the world. I want to assert that.

The family, society, nation, and world we live in cannot become the world of God's ideals as they are. We must fulfill the responsibilities entrusted to us with a longing to meet. Only by fulfilling those responsibilities can we meet the one we long for. After meeting, how should we face Him?

When Mary Magdalene tried to hold onto the resurrected Jesus, He refused. This was because Mary Magdalene had not yet walked the path she needed to take and had not prepared the offering she needed to bring. Those who have not fulfilled their responsibilities and have not prepared their offerings cannot appear before Jesus; this is the lesson Jesus teaches us there. Therefore, we must prepare our offerings in the victorious form of having walked the path we must take and fought the battles we must fight.

What is the offering here? You yourselves must become the offering. God will give to you to the extent that you become the offering. And to that extent, God will meet you.

So after you have walked the path and met the Father, what must you do? You must receive the Father's love. After participating in the final wedding feast of the bride and bridegroom and having a joyful reunion, what must you do? You must receive the Father's love. This is the hope of humanity. In the end, what remains is to receive love.

**Qualification to Become the Protagonist of Heaven**

To receive this love, I have walked the path of death, any difficult path, and the path of suffering. I have strived to love even Satan and have fought to become a sacrifice for a dying life. I have taken on the love that the Father wanted to express to humanity on earth, and I have poured out all my heart to those who long for love. "Father! Please love me!" 

You must welcome that hour when heaven can respond to your one plea.

The Jesus you believe in walked the path of tears for over 30 years. He crossed the peaks of sorrow and death. And after resurrecting, He said to God, "Father, I have come. I have understood the heart of the Father for 4,000 years, and I have come here as a sacrifice to introduce that heart." When He calls out "Father!" God forgot His dignity and held onto Jesus, weeping tears of joy. That moment was when the lost child was found, and the bond between heaven and earth was established. Christians do not know that at such a moment, God forgot His dignity and held onto Jesus, weeping tears of sorrow and joy.

You too must appear before the Father in the end, saying, "I have come the way you called me, and I believe in the words that say we will meet. Father, now embrace me in Your loving arms." You must be able to say this. And so, you must receive the blessing of being embraced in the arms of love, where the Father raises His hands and blesses you to live in eternal love! Only then will the conclusion of our hope, the ideal garden, that is, the construction of heaven, be realized.

You must understand that the construction of heaven begins with the completion of each individual.

Jesus fought for such an ideal, our ancestors sought this ideal, and today many people walking the path of virtue are heading toward this purpose.

So what is the heart you must resolve? You must have the desire to go and the desire to meet, but those are all passing things, things that fallen humans must indemnify. We must have a heart that wants to receive God's love even more than that. And we must manifest as the eternal embodiment of the love that God has stored up since eternity.

Thus, when God finds His beloved sons and daughters of love and boasts about them before all creation, before all the people of the world, and even before Satan, you must be able to say, "Yes, I am the fruit of love you sought, the protagonist of the garden of love you wanted to establish as your ideal."

You must become a being who can receive God's true love without dying, combining spirit and flesh, and who can build the ideal of heaven on earth and become the second heavenly heir of God who can govern that ideal kingdom of heaven, so that all creation and even wicked Satan will testify and bow their heads to you. Only then can you become the protagonist of heaven and the sons and daughters of heaven.

Matthew 5:33-48  
<Prayer> Beloved Father! The short life of humans seeking You may seem simple, but it is complicated, and we cannot help but walk such a path of life. We earnestly hope and wish that You will guide us to be blessed sons and daughters who can spend the rest of our lives in Your embrace, enduring today and tomorrow.

In this world today, we know that we are not the only ones living; there are countless satans surrounding us. We know that these satans have presented cunning battles and conditions of accusation before You for 6,000 years, and we understand that You have worked hard to protect us from them. Because it has replaced the world of heart, there is no development. Whether thousands of years ago or millions of years in the future, there is no development. The heart of a parent loving a child, the heart of a couple loving each other, the heart of loving one's kin and relatives—these feelings do not develop. Holding onto that one feeling can represent the whole, can replace completeness, and that one feeling can represent the happiness of the whole.

So, where is the highest happiness of life, and where is the ultimate resting place? If God exists as a subject, we can claim to be His children and call Him Father; it is also the place where God can call us His children. If such movements occur on a static foundation, from that moment on, the human world is a happy world, and it cannot be seen as anything other than the greatest successful world humanity has longed for.

For this reason, anyone who has come out with any religious ideology has been working to fulfill a feeling towards good. Jesus also came to this earth, calling God Father and declaring that He is one with God. No one has proclaimed a greater fact than this throughout history. And He referred to Himself as the bridegroom and humanity as the bride, and even further, He called them friends. He also referred to them as people and disciples.

He moved the overall emotional feelings of humanity and claimed the value of His subjectivity with all elements. No historical religious leader has made claims like Jesus. Jesus looked at the entire universe with a static heart, and when dealing with historical figures, He did not treat them flatly but with a historical heart. However, a conflict arose here. We must understand that this contradictory phenomenon appeared because it was a fallen world.

Jesus said to love me more than anyone else. This statement was a bombshell declaration in front of a world that had established habitual relationships and static connections until now; it was a revolutionary claim. Why? Because when Jesus looked at humanity with the heart of love flowing in His own heart, He could view it from the perspective of God's heart, who created the beginning and the end and passed through all human feelings. Until that time, the love that humanity had for one another was not recognized as the original love from heaven. That is why He made such statements.

Everything that appeared before Jesus, who made such claims, was an enemy. Everything was an enemy. Therefore, the steps He took were sorrowful steps. Yet, no one knew of that sorrow. No one understood the sorrow He felt when He was nailed to the cross on Golgotha, in front of His enemies. No one knew the joyful heart He looked upon with hope and expectation.

However, even at that time, Jesus thought that the sorrow of God, who created the infinite universe, while looking at fallen humanity, would be an infinite sorrow. God is not one who created everything and has hopes within limited bounds. If God is one who sighs over the fall of humanity, if He regrets having created humanity, then we must understand that God's sorrow is an infinite sorrow that we, with our emotions, cannot comprehend even after millions of years of thought.

On the other hand, we must understand that before God's heart was stained with infinite sorrow, it was a heart filled with infinite joy, longing for humanity. For this reason, Jesus did not succumb to infinite sorrow but sought to rise above it and find infinite joy. So what was the reason Jesus could hold onto that heart and fight on? He knew that even if he was expelled from the family of Joseph and faced unspeakable hardships, there was a sorrow greater than that sorrow. He knew that even if he was driven out by the nation and labeled a heretic by the church, there was a sorrow beyond that sorrow. Furthermore, he knew that even when he was rejected and pushed away by his beloved disciples, there was still a sorrow greater than that.

Even when He entered the place of being nailed to the cross, Jesus knew that there was a sorrow greater than the sorrow He felt at that moment, which allowed Him to pray for His enemies. At that time, Jesus understood that there was a heart of greater sorrow, a history of greater sorrow, and a standard of greater sorrow remaining.

To become a warrior seeking the heart of heaven

So why did God forsake Jesus but not forsake the world? Why could He not abandon His enemies even while giving Jesus to the cross? It was to testify that there was sorrow greater than Jesus' death.

We, the fallen, must seek this infinite ceiling and experience the historical heart that has protected and guided us, and we must appear before God in a victorious form. When you look at the society you live in, this world is not a world of joy. The history of humanity is a history of sorrow. Because the history of humanity did not start as a history of joy but as a history of sorrow, today’s history of humanity has become a history of sorrow.

When you see an individual crying out in their sorrow, you may feel sympathy. However, do not take pleasure in sympathizing with your own personal sorrows or advising others. Beyond the individual, there are sorrows of families, nations, the world, and even the heavens that are connected to us.

You may often cry out with your personal grievances, your personal misfortunes, your personal difficulties, and the sorrows that pierce your heart. However, there are sorrows greater than your personal sorrow remaining in families, societies, nations, the world, and the heavens.

Now, if we are to become warriors seeking the heart of heaven, we must feel our own sorrows but also be able to feel the ultimate sorrows. We must consider whether the rejections, betrayals, and injustices we face in our life journey are the final things in seeking that ceiling. There are sorrows beyond the sorrows tied among humans. If the Creator is great and high, it is natural that His ideals are great and high, and His goodness is great and high. We must not forget that in front of that heart, which longs for that goodness and ideal, there is a sorrow that takes the place of the great and high ideals, occupying the position of an infinite object.

In seeking that ceiling, we must not weep and shed tears centered around ourselves, starting from ourselves to achieve results for ourselves. Those who do so will perish holding onto themselves. Those who hold onto their families will perish with their families; those who hold onto their nations will perish with their nations; those who hold onto the world will perish with the world.

So what should we hold onto and weep for? We must become people who can hold onto the ceiling and weep. We must become people who can feel God's sorrow as our sorrow and God's difficulties as our difficulties.

As fallen humans, we must walk the sorrowful historical path toward Golgotha, knowing that the pain you feel today and the sorrows you endure are not the end. They are not the end.

For Jesus, who understood this, praying for His enemies was not a problem. Even if there were greater peaks of sorrow, He felt that He must fulfill the mission of a heavenly son beyond those peaks of sorrow. That is why Jesus could step over the peak of death. We must understand that it was with such a shock of heart that He could forgive His enemies on the cross and overcome death.

So what is the step of religion seeking? God established religion to introduce good and precious things to humanity, but humanity has had to walk difficult and sorrowful paths instead of good and precious steps.

I exist for whom?

The heavens have labored and grieved for 6,000 years, which is not introduced in any religious scripture. However, it has meticulously introduced goodness and the blessed land where we can live.

So why did heaven take such measures? It is because heaven loves us. Because heaven loves us, it has come to us through this means. While humanity seeks heaven, joy does not come all at once in a day. Joy can be found only after passing through the path of sorrow.

If there is someone on earth who hopes for heaven, and if there is someone on earth who wishes to become a true son or daughter of heaven, they must be someone who can raise their hands in prayer and weep, saying, "Let me shed tears for God's 6,000 years of sorrow in my lifetime." They must be someone who can cry out with their life, risking everything for heaven, earth, and all creation.

The person who discovers that the Father is in a sorrowful position, not in a good, beautiful, precious, proud, and glorious position, will become the protagonist of goodness that the Father seeks. You must understand that becoming a true son or daughter of God is essential.

If heaven has eyes and sheds tears, it would have shed more tears than any lake or river on this earth, grieving to the extent that there would be no place to fill the tears in heaven and earth. Therefore, a person who can experience God's sorrow will feel that when they look at the mountains, they are the peaks of heaven's labor and pain; when they see the sea, they will feel it as God's tears; and when they look at the plants, they will feel it as God's worries. When they gaze upon the vast, deep, and wide universe, they will see that while all phenomena are beautiful, that beauty is a condition of sorrow for God, who sees that beauty does not have a direct relationship with humanity. We must understand that God is searching for sons and daughters who can feel such things and call upon the Father with such emotions.

A true filial child is not someone who only appears as a filial son or daughter by rejoicing and enjoying with the Father. Such a person is not a filial child. Only those who can take on the sorrow of the Father and the difficulties of the Father can be called filial children.

If this is true for humans, it is the same for heaven. Because we live in a fallen world where relationships cannot be tied with joy, we must go through the paths of sorrow and hardship. Even if our hands become calloused and our bodies become tired and torn, we must have the heart to run toward heaven. 

When we cry out, "Father!" in such deep sorrow that we cannot plead with any human on this earth, that one hour is the time we can connect with the lost ceiling.

Humans must recover such times and have moments in their lives where they bow their heads and shed tears before heaven. And the moment when sorrow disappears from that heart and joy and peace can be sung is the moment heaven comes, the moment heaven can smile, and the moment heaven can raise its hands and bless us as His sons and daughters.

Fallen humanity must go. We must stop the steps we have taken until today and walk the new path of sorrow. Humanity, which has not known that heaven has walked the path of sorrow for 6,000 years to protect us, must lament for itself. We must lament for the families, nations, and world we live in.

Unless we follow the footsteps of Jesus, who prayed for His enemies while thinking of God's sorrow over the peak of death, we cannot feel God's heart of labor and God's heart of sorrow as humans on this earth.

If we cannot resolve the sorrow that pierces God's heart, then the eternal joy, eternal goodness, and eternal happiness within God can never be connected to humanity on this earth.

Today, you must reconsider your position. There have been many times you have shed tears. But where have those tears gone? Reflect once more. Your hands are moving a lot to live for yourselves. However, you must stop and think for whom these hands are moving, for whom these steps are struggling, and for whom this body and heart are longing and seeking. You must remember that you are in a position of historical sorrow, and you must feel that you cannot help but seek a day of hope again, awakening anew and criticizing your past life. You must lament that you have not become what heaven desires and that you have not established a connection with heaven.

Will you always feel that you have no face before your family, no face before your nation, and no face before the world? If such feelings arise from your heart, then whether you look at your family, your nation, the world, or heaven, it will be tears. If such things do not occur in your life, you must understand that you cannot find God's goodness, God's joy, and God's happiness hidden beneath the black curtain of God's heart.

Now, while living, we must analyze whether we are living for ourselves, knowing that there is one who protects us, whether we know it or not, who protects us even in difficult situations. We must learn to look to that one who protects us regardless of our circumstances.
